  {Quī regis Isrāēlem, intende, quī dēdūcis velut ovem Jōsēfum. Quī sedēs super cherubim, manifestāre.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Cōram Efraim, Benjamin, et Manasse excitā potentiam tuam, et venī ut salvōs faciās nōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Deus, converte nōs, et ostende faciem tuam, et salvī erimus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Domine Deus virtūtum, ¿~quousque īrāsceris super ōrātiōnem servī tuī~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {¿~Cibābis nōs pāne lacrimārum, et pōtum dabis nōbīs in lacrimīs in mensūrā~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Posuistī nōs in contrādictiōnem vīcīnīs nostrīs, et inimīcī nostrī subsannāvērunt nōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Deus virtūtum, converte nōs, et ostende faciem tuam, et salvī erimus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Vīneam dē Aegiptō transtulistī~; ēiēcistī Gentēs, et plantāvistī eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Dux itineris fuistī in conspectū ejus~; plantāvistī rādīcēs ejus, et implēvit terram.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Operuit montēs umbra ejus, et arbusta ejus cedrōs Deī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Extendit palmitēs suōs usque ad mare, et usque ad flūmen propāginēs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {¿~Ut quid dēstruxistī māceriam ejus, et vindēmiant eam omnēs, quī praetergrediuntur viam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Extermināvit eam aper dē silvā, et singulāris ferus dēpāstus est eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Deus virtūtum, convertere~; respice dē caelō, et vidē, et vīsitā vīneam istam,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {et perfice eam quam plantāvit dexterā tuā, et super fīlium hominis quem confirmāvistī tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Incensa ignī et suffossa~; ab increpātiōne vultūs tuī perībunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Fīat manus tua super virum dexterae tuae, et super fīlium hominis, quem confirmāvistī tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Et nōn discēdimus ā tē~; vīvificābis nōs, et nōmen tuum invocābimus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Domine Deus virtūtum, converte nōs, et ostende faciem tuam, et salvī erimus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{80}{In fīnem prō torculāribus Āsāfō}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Exsultāte Deō adjūtōrī nostrō~; jūbilāte Deō Jācōbis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Sūmite psalmum, et date timpanum~; psaltērium jūcundum cum cittarā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Būcināte in neomēniā tubā, in insignī diē sōlemnitātis vestrae,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {quia praeceptum in Isrāēle est, et jūdicium Deō Jācōbis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Testimōnium in Jōsēfō posuit illud, quum exīret dē terrā Aegiptī~; linguam quam nōn nōverat, audīvit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Dīvertit ab oneribus dorsum ejus~; manūs ejus in cofinō servīvērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {In trībulātiōne invocāvistī mē, et līberāvī tē~; exaudīvī tē in absconditō tempestātis~; probāvī tē apud aquam contrādictiōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Audī, populus meus, et contestābor tē~; Isrāel, sī audīverīs mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Nōn erit in tē deus recens, neque adōrābis deum aliēnum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Egō enim sum Dominus Deus tuus, quī ēduxī tē dē terrā Aegiptī~; dīlātā os tuum, et implēbō illud.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Et nōn audīvit populus meus vōcem meam, et Isrāel nōn intendit mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Et dīmīsī eōs secundum dēsīderia cordis eōrum~; ībunt in adinventiōnibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Sī populus meus audīvisset mē, Isrāel sī in viīs meīs ambulāsset,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {prō nihilō forsitan inimīcōs eōrum humiliāssem, et super trībulantēs eōs mīsissem manum meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Inimīcī Dominī mentītī sunt eī, et erit tempus eōrum in saecula.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Et cibāvit eōs ex adipe frūmentī, et dē petrā, melle saturāvit eōs.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{11}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{81}{Psalmus Āsāfō}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Deus stetit in sinagōgā deōrum, in mediō autem deōs dījūdicat.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {¿~Usquequō jūdicātis inīquitātem, et faciēs peccātōrum sūmitis~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Jūdicāte egēnō et pūpillō~; humilem et pauperem jūstificāte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Ēripite pauperem, et egēnum dē manū peccātōris līberāte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Nescīvērunt, neque intellexērunt~; in tenebrīs ambulant~; movēbuntur omnia fundāmenta terrae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Egō dixī, «~Deī estis, et fīliī excelsī omnēs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Vōs autem sīcut hominēs moriēminī, et sīcut ūnus dē principibus cadētis.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Surge, Deus, jūdicā terram, quoniam tū hērēditābis in omnibus gentibus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{82}{Canticum psalmī Āsāfō}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Deus, ¿~quis similis erit tibī~? Nē taceās, neque compescāris, Deus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {quoniam ecce inimīcī tuī sonuērunt, et quī ōdērunt tē, extulērunt caput.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Super populum tuum malignāvērunt consilium, et cōgitāvērunt adversus sanctōs tuōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Dixērunt, «~Venīte, et disperdāmus eōs dē gente, et nōn memorētur nōmen Isrāēlis ultrā.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Quoniam cōgitāvērunt ūnanimiter~; simul adversum tē testāmentum disposuērunt,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {tabernācula Idūmaeōrum et Ismahelītae, Moāb et Aggarēnī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Gebal et Ammon et Amālec, aliēnigenae cum habitantibus Tīrī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {etenim Assur vēnit cum illīs, factī sunt in adjūtōrium fīliīs Lōtis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Fac illīs sīcut Midiānī et Siserae, sīcut Jābin in torrente Cīsōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Disperīvērunt in Endōre~; factī sunt ut stercus terrae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Pōne principēs eōrum sīcut Oreb et Zeb et Zēbach et Salmunna~; omnēs principēs eōrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {quī dixērunt, «~Hērēditāte possideāmus sanctuārium Deī.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Deus meus, pōne illōs ut rotam, et sīcut stipulam ante faciem ventī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Sīcut ignis quī combūrit silvam, et sīcut flamma combūrens montēs,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {ita persequeris illōs in tempestāte tuā, et in īrā tuā turbābis eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Implē faciēs eōrum ignōminiā, et quaerent nōmen tuum, Domine.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Ērubēscant, et conturbentur in saeculum saeculī, et confundantur, et periant.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Et cognōscant quia nōmen tibī Dominus~; tū sōlus Altissimus in omnī terrā.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{83}{In fīnem prō torculāribus fīliīs Coris Psalmus}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Quam dīlecta tabernācula tua Domine virtūtum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Concupīscit, et dēficit anima mea in ātria Dominī~; cor meum et carō mea exsultāvērunt in Deum vīvum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Etenim passer invēnit sibī domum, et turtur nīdum sibī, ubi pōnat pullōs suōs~; altāria tua, Domine virtūtum, rex meus, et Deus meus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Beātī quī habitant in domū tuā, Domine~; in saecula saeculōrum laudābunt tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Beātus vir cujus est auxilium ā tē~; ascensiōnēs in corde suō disposuit,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {in valle lacrimārum, in locō quem posuit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Etenim benedictiōnem dabit lēgislātor~; ībunt dē virtūte in virtūtem~; vidēbitur Deus deōrum in Siōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Domine Deus virtūtum, exaudī ōrātiōnem meam~; auribus percipe, Deus Jācōbis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Prōtector noster, aspice, Deus, et respice in faciem chrīstī tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Quia melior est diēs ūna in ātriīs tuīs super millia~; ēlēgī abiectus esse in domū Deī meī magis quam habitāre in tabernāculīs peccātōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Quia misericordiam et vēritātem dīligit Deus~; grātiam et glōriam dabit Dominus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Nōn prīvābit bonīs eōs quī ambulant in innocentiā~; Domine virtūtum, beātus homō quī spērat in tē.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{84}{In fīnem fīliīs Coris psalmus}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Benedixistī, Domine, terram tuam~; āvertistī captīvitātem Jācōbis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Remīsistī inīquitātem plēbis tuae~; operuistī omnia peccāta eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Mītigāvistī omnem īram tuam~; āvertistī ab īrā indignātiōnis tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Converte nōs, Deus salūtāris noster, et āverte īram tuam ā nōbīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {¿~Numquid in aeternum īrāsceris nōbīs, aut extendēs īram tuam ā generātiōne in generātiōnem~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Deus, tū conversus vīvificābis nōs, et plēbs tua laetābitur in tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Ostende nōbīs, Domine, misericordiam tuam, et salūtāre tuum dā nōbīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Audiem quid loquātur in mē Dominus Deus, quoniam loquētur pācem in plēbem suam, et super sanctōs suōs, et in eōs quī convertuntur ad cor.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Vērumtamen prope timentēs eum salūtāre ipsīus, ut inhabitet glōria in terrā nostrā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Misericordia et vēritās obviāvērunt sibī~; jūstitia et pax ōsculātae sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Vēritās dē terrā orta est, et jūstitia dē caelō prōspexit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Etenim Dominus dabit benignitātem, et terra nostra dabit fructum suum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Jūstitia ante eum ambulābit, et pōnet in viā gressūs suōs.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{12}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{85}{Ōrātiō ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Inclīnā, Domine, aurem tuam, et exaudī mē, quoniam inops et pauper sum egō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Custōdī animam meam, quoniam sanctus sum~; salvum fac servum tuum, Deus meus, spērantem in tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Miserēre meī, Domine, quoniam ad tē clāmāvī tōtā diē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Laetificā animam servī tuī, quoniam ad tē, Domine, animam meam levāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quoniam tū, Domine, suāvis et mītis, et multae misericordiae omnibus invocantibus tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Auribus percipe, Domine, ōrātiōnem meam, et intende vōcī dēprecātiōnis meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {In diē trībulātiōnis meae clāmāvī ad tē, quia exaudīvistī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Nōn est similis tuī in deīs, Domine, et nōn est secundum opera tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Omnēs gentēs quāscumque fēcistī venient, et adōrābunt cōram tē, Domine, et glōrificābunt nōmen tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quoniam magnus es tū, et faciens mīrābilia~; tū es Deus sōlus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Dēdūc mē, Domine, in viā tuā, et ingredier in vēritāte tuā~; laetētur cor meum ut timeat nōmen tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Confitēbor tibī, Domine Deus meus, in tōtō corde meō, et glōrificābō nōmen tuum in aeternum~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {quia misericordia tua magna est super mē, et ērūvistī animam meam ex infernō inferiōrī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Deus, inīquī insurrexērunt super mē, et sinagōga potentium quaesīvērunt animam meam, et nōn prōposuērunt tē in conspectū suō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Et tū, Domine Deus, miserātor et misericors~; patiens, et multae misericordiae, et vērax.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Respice in mē, et miserēre meī~; dā imperium tuum puerō tuō, et salvum fac fīlium ancillae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Fac mēcum signum in bonum, ut videant quī ōdērunt mē, et confundantur~; quoniam tū, Domine, adjūvistī mē, et consōlātus es mē.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{86}{Fīliīs Coris psalmus canticī}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Fundāmenta ejus in montibus sanctīs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {dīligit Dominus portās Siōnis super omnia tabernācula Jācōbis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Glōriōsa dicta sunt dē tē, cīvitās Deī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Memor erō Rahab, et Babilōnis scientium mē. Ecce aliēnigenae et Tīrus et populus Aetiōpum, hī fuērunt illīc.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {¿~Numquid Siōn dīcet, «~Homō et homō nātus est in eā, et ipse fundāvit eam Altissimus~»~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Dominus narrābit in scrīptūrīs populōrum, et principum, hōrum, quī fuērunt in eā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Sīcut laetantium omnium habitātiō est in tē.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{87}{Canticum psalmī fīliīs Coris in fīnem prō Māhalatō ad respondendum intellēctus Hēmānī Ezrāhītae}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Domine, Deus salūtis meae, in diē clāmāvī, et nocte cōram tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Intret in conspectū tuō ōrātiō mea~; inclīnā aurem tuam ad precem meam,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {quia replēta est malīs anima mea, et vīta mea infernō appropinquāvit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Aestimātus sum cum dēscendentibus in lacum~; factus sum sīcut homō sine adjūtōriō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {inter mortuōs līber, Sīcut vulnerātī dormientēs in sepulchrīs, quōrum nōn es memor amplius, et ipsī dē manū tuā repulsī sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Posuērunt mē in lacū inferiōrī, in tenebrōsīs, et in umbrā mortis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Super mē confirmātus est furor tuus, et omnēs fluctūs tuōs induxistī super mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Longē fēcistī nōtōs meōs ā mē~; posuērunt mē abōminātiōnem sibī. Trāditus sum, et nōn ēgrediēbar~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {oculī meī languērunt prae inopiā. Clāmāvī ad tē Domine tōtā diē~; expandī ad tē manūs meās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {¿~Numquid mortuīs faciēs mīrābilia, aut medicī suscitābunt et confitēbuntur tibī~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {¿~Numquid narrābit aliquis in sepulchrō misericordiam tuam, et vēritātem tuam in perditiōne~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {¿~Numquid cognōscentur in tenebrīs mīrābilia tua, et jūstitia tua in terrā oblīviōnis~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Et egō ad tē, Domine, clāmāvī, et māne ōrātiō mea praeveniet tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {¿~Ut quid, Domine, repellis ōrātiōnem meam~; āvertis faciem tuam ā mē~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Pauper sum egō, et in labōribus ā juventūte meā~; exaltātus autem, humiliātus sum et conturbātus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {In mē transīvērunt īrae tuae, et terrōrēs tuī conturbāvērunt mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Circumdedērunt mē sīcut aqua tōtā diē~; circumdedērunt mē simul.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Ēlongāvistī ā mē amīcum et proximum, et nōtōs meōs ā miseriā.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{12}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{88}{Intellēctus Ētānī Ezrāhītae}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Misericordiās Dominī in aeternum cantābō~; in generātiōnem et generātiōnem adnuntiābō vēritātem tuam in ōre meō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {quoniam dixistī, «~In aeternum misericordia aedificābitur in caelīs.~»Praeparābitur vēritās tua in eīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {«~Disposuī testāmentum ēlectīs meīs, jūrāvī Dāvid servō meō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {‹ Usque in aeternum praeparābō sēmen tuum, et aedificābō in generātiōnem et generātiōnem sēdem tuam. ›~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Confitēbuntur caelī mīrābilia tua, Domine, etenim vēritātem tuam in ecclēsiā sanctōrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {¿~quoniam quis in nūbibus aequābitur Dominō~; similis erit Deō in fīliīs Deī~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Deus, quī glōrificātur in consiliō sanctōrum, magnus et terribilis super omnēs quī in circumitū ejus sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Domine Deus virtūtum, ¿~quis similis tibī~? Potens es, Domine, et vēritās tua in circumitū tuō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Tū domināris potestātī maris~; mōtum autem fluctuum ejus tū mītigās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Tū humiliāvistī sīcut vulnerātum, superbum~; in bracchiō virtūtis tuae dispersistī inimīcōs tuōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Tuī sunt caelī, et tua est terra~; orbem terrae et plēnitūdinem ejus tū fundāvistī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Aquilōnem et mare tū creāvistī~; Tābor et Hermōn in nōmine tuō exsultābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Tuum bracchium cum potentiā~; firmētur manus tua, et exaltētur dextera tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Jūstitia et jūdicium praeparātiō sēdis tuae~; misericordia et vēritās praecēdent faciem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Beātus populus, quī scit jūbilātiōnem~; Domine, in lūmine vultūs tuī ambulābunt,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {et in nōmine tuō exsultābunt tōtā diē, et in jūstitiā tuā exaltābuntur,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {quoniam glōria virtūtis eōrum tū es, et in benēplacitō tuō exaltābitur cornū nostrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {quia Dominī est assumptiō nostra, et sanctī Isrāēlis rēgis nostrī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Tunc locūtus es in vīsiōne sanctīs tuīs, et dixistī, «~Posuī adjūtōrium in potente, et exaltāvī ēlectum dē plēbe meā.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Invēnī Dāvid servum meum~; oleō sanctō meō unxī eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Manus enim mea auxiliābitur eī, et bracchium meum confortābit eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Nihil prōficiet inimīcus in eō, et fīlius inīquitātis nōn appōnet nocēre eī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Et concīdem ā faciē ipsīus inimīcōs ejus, et odientēs eum in fugam convertem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Et vēritās mea et misericordia mea cum ipsō, et in nōmine meō exaltābitur cornū ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Et pōnem in marī manum ejus, et in flūminibus dexteram ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Ipse invocābit mē, «~Pater meus es tū, Deus meus, et susceptor salūtis meae.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {Et egō prīmōgenitum pōnem illum, excelsum prae rēgibus terrae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {In aeternum servābō illī misericordiam meam, et testāmentum meum fidēle ipsī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Et pōnem in saeculum saeculī sēmen ejus, et tronum ejus sīcut diēs caelī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Sī autem dērelīquerint fīliī ejus lēgem meam, et in jūdiciīs meīs nōn ambulāverint,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}32}
  {sī jūstitiās meās prōfānāverint, et mandāta mea nōn custōdīverint,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}33}
  {vīsitābō in virgā inīquitātēs eōrum, et in verberibus peccāta eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}34}
  {Misericordiam autem meam nōn dispergem ab eō, neque nocēbō in vēritāte meā,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}35}
  {neque prōfānābō testāmentum meum, et quae prōcēdunt dē labiīs meīs nōn faciam irrita.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}36}
  {Semel jūrāvī in sanctō meō, sī Dāvidī mentier~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}37}
  {sēmen ejus in aeternum manēbit, et tronus ejus sīcut sōl in conspectū meō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}38}
  {et sīcut lūna perfecta in aeternum, et testis in caelō fidēlis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}39}
  {Tū vērō repulistī et dēspexistī~; distulistī chrīstum tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}40}
  {Ēvertistī testāmentum servī tuī~; prōfānāvistī in terrā sanctuārium ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}41}
  {Dēstruxistī omnēs sēpēs ejus~; posuistī firmāmentum ejus formīdinem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}42}
  {Dīripuērunt eum omnēs transientēs viam~; factus est opprobrium vīcīnīs suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}43}
  {Exaltāvistī dexteram dēprimentium eum~; laetificāvistī omnēs inimīcōs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}44}
  {Āvertistī adjūtōrium gladiī ejus, et nōn es auxiliātus eī in bellō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}45}
  {Dēstruxistī eum ab ēmundātiōne, et sēdem ejus in terram collīsistī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}46}
  {Minōrāvistī diēs temporis ejus~; perfūdistī eum confūsiōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}47}
  {¿~Usquequō, Domine, āvertis in fīnem~? ¿~Exardēscet sīcut ignis īra tua~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}48}
  {Memorāre quae mea substantia~; ¿~numquid enim vānē constitūvistī omnēs fīliōs hominum~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}49}
  {¿~Quis est homō quī vīvet et nōn vidēbit mortem, ēruet animam suam dē manū inferī~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}50}
  {¿~Ubi sunt misericordiae tuae antīquae, Domine, sīcut jūrāvistī Dāvid in vēritāte tuā~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}51}
  {Memor estō, Domine, opprobriī servōrum tuōrum, quod continuī in sinū meō, multārum gentium,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}52}
  {quod exprobrāvērunt inimīcī tuī, Domine, quod exprobrāvērunt commūtātiōnem chrīstī tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}53}
  {Benedictus Dominus in aeternum. Fīat, fīat.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{12}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{89}{Ōrātiō Mōsīs hominis Deī}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Domine, refugium factus es nōbīs ā generātiōne in generātiōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Priusquam montēs fierent, aut formārētur terra et orbis, ā saeculō et usque in saeculum tū es Deus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Nē āvertās hominem in humilitātem. Et dixistī, «~Convertiminī, fīliī hominum.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quoniam mille annī ante oculōs tuōs tamquam diēs hesterna quae praeterīvit, et custōdia in nocte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quae prō nihilō habentur, eōrum annī erunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Māne sīcut herba transiat~; māne flōriat, et transiat~; vespere dēcidat, indūret, et ārēscat.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Quia dēfēcimus in īrā tuā, et in furōre tuō turbātī sumus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Posuistī inīquitātēs nostrās in conspectū tuō~; saeculum nostrum in illūminātiōne vultūs tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Quoniam omnēs diēs nostrī dēfēcērunt, et in īrā tuā dēfēcimus. Annī nostrī sīcut arānea meditābuntur~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {diēs annōrum nostrōrum in ipsīs, septuāgintā annī. Sī autem in potentātibus octōgintā annī, et amplius eōrum labor et dolor~; quoniam supervēnit mansuētūdō, et corripiēmur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {¿~Quis nōvit potestātem īrae tuae, et prae timōre tuō īram tuam dīnumerāre~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Dexteram tuam sīc nōtam fac, et ērudītōs corde in sapientiā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Convertere, Domine~; ¿~usquequō~? Et dēprecābilis estō super servōs tuōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Replētī sumus māne misericordiā tuā, et exsultāvimus et dēlectātī sumus omnibus diēbus nostrīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Laetātī sumus prō diēbus quibus nōs humiliāvistī~; annīs quibus vīdimus mala.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Respice in servōs tuōs, et in opera tua, et dīrige fīliōs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Et sit splendor Dominī Deī nostrī super nōs, et opera manuum nostrārum dīrige super nōs, et opus manuum nostrārum dīrige.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{90}{Laus canticī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Quī habitat in adjūtōriō Altissimī, in prōtectiōne Deī caelī commorābitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Dīcet Dominō, «~Susceptor meus es tū, et refugium meum~; Deus meus, spērābō in eum.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quoniam ipse līberāvit mē dē laqueō vēnantium, et ā verbō asperō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Scapulīs suīs obumbrābit tibī, et sub pennīs ejus spērābis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Scūtō circumdabit tē vēritās ejus~; nōn timēbis ā timōre nocturnō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {ā sagittā volante in diē, ā negōtiō perambulante in tenebrīs, ab incursū, et daemoniō merīdiānō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Cadent ā latere tuō mille, et decem millia ā dextrīs tuīs, ad tē autem nōn appropinquābit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Vērumtamen oculīs tuīs consīderābis, et retribūtiōnem peccātōrum vidēbis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Quoniam tū es, Domine, spēs mea~; Altissimum posuistī refugium tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Nōn accēdet ad tē malum, et flagellum nōn appropinquābit tabernāculō tuō~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {quoniam angelīs suīs mandāvit dē tē, ut custōdiant tē in omnibus viīs tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {In manibus portābunt tē, nē forte offendās ad lapidem pedem tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Super aspidem et basiliscum ambulābis, et conculcābis leōnem et dracōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Quoniam in mē spērāvit, līberābō eum~; prōtegem eum, quoniam cognōvit nōmen meum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Clāmābit ad mē, et egō exaudiem eum~; cum ipsō sum in trībulātiōne~; ēripiem eum et glōrificābō eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Longitūdine diērum replēbō eum, et ostendem illī salūtāre meum.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{13}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{91}{Psalmus canticī in diē sabbatī}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Bonum est confitērī Dominō, et psallere nōminī tuō, Altissime,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {ad adnuntiandum māne misericordiam tuam, et vēritātem tuam per noctem,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {in decachordō, psaltēriō, cum canticō in cittarā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quia dēlectāvistī mē, Domine, in factūrā tuā, et in operibus manuum tuārum exsultābō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Quam magnificāta sunt opera tua, Domine. Nimis prōfundae factae sunt cōgitātiōnēs tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Vir insapiens nōn cognōscet, et stultus nōn intelleget haec.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Quum exortī fuerint peccātōrēs sīcut foenum, et appāruerint omnēs quī operantur inīquitātem, ut interiant in saeculum saeculī~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {tū autem Altissimus in aeternum, Domine.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quoniam ecce inimīcī tuī, Domine, quoniam ecce inimīcī tuī perībunt, et dispergentur omnēs quī operantur inīquitātem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Et exaltābitur sīcut ūnicornis cornū meum, et senectūs mea in misericordiā ūberī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Et dēspexit oculus meus inimīcōs meōs, et in insurgentibus in mē malignantibus audiet auris mea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Jūstus ut palma flōrēbit~; sīcut cedrus Libanī multiplicābitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Plantātī in domū Dominī, in ātriīs domus Deī nostrī flōrēbunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Adhūc multiplicābuntur in senectā ūberī, et bene patientēs erunt,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {ut adnuntient quoniam rectus Dominus Deus noster, et nōn est inīquitās in eō.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{92}{Laus canticī ipsi Dāvīdis in diē ante sabbatum quandō fundāta est terra}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Dominus regnāvit, decōrem indūtus est~; indūtus est Dominus fortitūdinem, et praecinxit sē. Etenim firmāvit orbem terrae, quī nōn commovēbitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Parāta sēdēs tua ex tunc~; ā saeculō tū es.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Ēlevāvērunt flūmina, Domine, ēlevāvērunt flūmina vōcem suam~; ēlevāvērunt flūmina fluctūs suōs,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {ā vōcibus aquārum multārum. Mīrābilēs ēlātiōnēs maris~; mīrābilis in altīs Dominus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Testimōnia tua crēdibilia facta sunt nimis~; domum tuam decet sanctitūdō, Domine, in longitūdinem diērum.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{93}{Psalmus ipsī Dāvīdis quārtā sabbatī}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Deus ultiōnum Dominus~; Deus ultiōnum līberē ēgit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Exaltāre, quī jūdicās terram~; redde retribūtiōnem superbīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {¿~Usquequō peccātōrēs, Domine, usquequō peccātōrēs glōriābuntur~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {¿~Effābuntur et loquentur inīquitātem~; loquentur omnēs, quī operantur injūstitiam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Populum tuum, Domine, humiliāvērunt, et hērēditātem tuam vexāvērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Viduam et advenam interfēcērunt, et pūpillōs occīsērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Et dixērunt, «~Nōn vidēbit Dominus, nec intelleget Deus Jācōbis.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Intellegite, insapientēs in populō, et, stultī, aliquandō sapite.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Quī plantāvit aurem, ¿~nōn audiet~? Aut quī finxit oculum, ¿~nōn consīderat~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quī corripit gentēs, ¿~nōn arguet, quī docet hominem scientiam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Dominus scit cōgitātiōnēs hominum, quoniam vānae sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Beātus homō, quem tū ērudīverīs Domine, et dē lēge tuā docuerīs eum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {ut mītigēs eī ā diēbus malīs, dōnec fodiātur peccātōrī fovea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Quia nōn repellet Dominus plēbem suam, et hērēditātem suam nōn dērelinquet,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {quoadusque jūstitia convertātur in jūdicium, et quī juxtā illam omnēs quī rectō sunt corde.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {¿~Quis consurget mihī adversus malignantēs, aut quis stābit mēcum adversus operantēs inīquitātem~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Nisī quia Dominus adjūvit mē, paulō minus habitāsset in infernō anima mea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Sī dīcēbam, «~Mōtus est pēs meus~; misericordia tua, Domine, adjuvābat mē.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Secundum multitūdinem dolōrum meōrum in corde meō, consōlātiōnēs tuae laetificāvērunt animam meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {¿~Numquid adhaeret tibī sēdēs inīquitātis, quī fingis labōrem in praeceptō~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Captābunt in animam jūstī, et sanguinem innocentem condemnābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Et factus est mihī Dominus in refugium, et Deus meus in adjūtōrium speī meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Et reddet illīs inīquitātem ipsōrum, et in malitiā eōrum disperdet eōs~; disperdet illōs Dominus Deus noster.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{13}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{94}{Canticum ipsī Dāvīdis quandō domus aedificābātur post captivitátem}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Venīte, exsultēmus Dominō~; jūbilēmus Deō salūtārī nostrō~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {praeoccupēmus faciem ejus in confessiōne, et in psalmīs jūbilēmus eī~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {quoniam Deus magnus Dominus, et Rex magnus super omnēs deōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quia in manū ejus sunt omnēs fīnēs terrae, et altitūdinēs montium ipsīus sunt~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {quoniam ipsīus est mare, et ipse fēcit illud, et siccam manūs ejus formāvērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Venīte, adōrēmus et prōcidāmus, et plōrēmus ante Dominum quī fēcit nōs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {quia ipse est Dominus Deus noster, et nōs populus pāscuae ejus, et ovēs manūs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Hodiē sī vōcem ejus audīverītis, nōlīte obdūrāre corda vestra, sīcut in irrītātiōne, secundum diem tentātiōnis in dēsertō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {ubi tentāvērunt mē patrēs vestrī, probāvērunt mē, et vīdērunt opera mea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quadrāgintā annīs offensus fuī generātiōnī illī, et dixī, «~Semper hī errant corde.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Et istī nōn cognōvērunt viās meās~; ut jūrāvī in īrā meā, «~Sī introībunt in requiem meam.~»}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{95}{Laus canticī ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Cantāte Dominō canticum novum~; cantāte Dominō, omnis terra.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Cantāte Dominō, et benedīcite nōminī ejus~; adnuntiāte dē diē in diem salūtāre ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Adnuntiāte inter Gentēs glōriam ejus~; in omnibus populīs mīrābilia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quoniam magnus Dominus, et laudābilis nimis~; terribilis est super omnēs deōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quoniam omnēs deī Gentium daemonia~; Dominus autem caelōs fēcit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Confessiō et pulchritūdō in conspectū ejus~; sanctimōnia et magnificentia in sanctificātiōne ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Afferte Dominō, patriae gentium, afferte Dominō glōriam et honōrem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Afferte Dominō glōriam nōminī ejus~; tollite hostiās, et introīte in ātria ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Adōrāte Dominum in ātriō sanctō ejus~; commoveātur ā faciē ejus ūniversa terra.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Dīcite in Gentibus quia Dominus regnāvit. Etenim correxit orbem terrae quī nōn commovēbitur~; jūdicābit populōs in aequitāte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Laetentur caelī, et exsultet terra~; commoveātur mare, et plēnitūdō ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Gaudēbunt campī, et omnia quae in eīs sunt~; tunc exsultābunt omnia ligna silvārum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {ā faciē Dominī, quia venit, quoniam venit jūdicāre terram. Jūdicābit orbem terrae in aequitāte, et populōs in vēritāte suā.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{96}{Huic Dāvīdis quandō terra ejus restitūta est}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Dominus regnāvit~; exsultet terra~; laetentur insulae multae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Nūbēs et cālīgō in circumitū ejus~; jūstitia et jūdicium correctiō sēdis ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Ignis ante ipsum praecēdet, et inflammābit in circumitū inimīcōs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Illuxērunt fulgura ejus orbī terrae~; vīdit, et commōta est terra.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Montēs sīcut cēra fluxērunt ā faciē Dominī~; ā faciē Dominī omnis terrae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Adnuntiāvērunt caelī jūstitiam ejus, et vīdērunt omnēs populī glōriam ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Confundantur omnēs quī adōrant sculptilia, et quī glōriantur in simulācrīs suīs. Adōrāte eum omnēs angelī ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Audīvit, et laetāta est Siōn, et exsultāvērunt fīliae Jūdae propter jūdicia tua, Domine.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Quoniam tū Dominus altissimus super omnem terram~; nimis exaltātus es super omnēs deōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quī dīligitis Dominum, odītē malum~; custōdit Dominus animās sanctōrum suōrum~; dē manū peccātōris līberābit eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Lux orta est jūstō, et rectīs corde laetitia.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Laetāminī, jūstī, in Dominō, et confitēminī memoriae sanctificātiōnis ejus.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{13}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{97}{Psalmus ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Cantāte Dominō canticum novum, quia mīrābilia fēcit. Salvāvit sibī dextera ejus, et bracchium sanctum ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Nōtum fēcit Dominus salūtāre suum~; in conspectū gentium revēlāvit jūstitiam suam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Recordātus est misericordiae suae et vēritātis suae domuī Isrāēlis. Vīdērunt omnēs terminī terrae salūtāre Deī nostrī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Jūbilāte Deō omnis terra~; cantāte, et exsultāte, et psallite.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Psallite Dominō in cittarā, in cittarā et vōce psalmī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {In tubīs ductilibus et vōce tubae corneae, jūbilāte in conspectū rēgis Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Moveātur mare et plēnitūdō ejus~; orbis terrārum et quī habitant in eō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Flūmina plaudent manū~; simul montēs exsultābunt ā conspectū Dominī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {quoniam venit jūdicāre terram. Jūdicābit orbem terrārum in jūstitiā, et populōs in aequitāte.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{98}{Psalmus ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Dominus regnāvit~; īrāscantur populī. Quī sedet super cherūbīm~; moveātur terra.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Dominus in Siōne magnus, et excelsus super omnēs populōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Confiteantur nōminī tuō magnō, quoniam terribile et sanctum est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Et honor rēgis jūdicium dīligit~; tū parāvistī dīrectiōnēs~; jūdicium et jūstitiam in Jācōbe tū fēcistī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Exaltāte Dominum Deum nostrum, et adōrāte scabellum pedum ejus, quoniam sanctum est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Mōsēs et Aarōn in sacerdōtibus ejus, et Samuel inter eōs quī invocant nōmen ejus. Invocābant Dominum, et ipse exaudiēbat eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {In columnā nūbis loquēbātur ad eōs~; custōdiēbant testimōnia ejus, et praeceptum quod dedit illīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Domine Deus noster, tū exaudiēbās eōs~; Deus tū propitius fuistī eīs, et ulcīscens in omnēs adinventiōnēs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Exaltāte Dominum Deum nostrum, et adōrāte in monte sanctō ejus, quoniam sanctus Dominus Deus noster.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{99}{Psalmus in confessiōne}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Jūbilāte Deō, omnis terra~; servīte Dominō in laetitiā. Introīte in conspectū ejus in exsultātiōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Scītōte quoniam Dominus ipse est Deus. Ipse fēcit nōs, et nōn ipsī nōs~; populus ejus, et ovēs pāscuae ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Introīte portās ejus in confessiōne, ātria ejus in himnīs. Confitēminī illī~; laudāte nōmen ejus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {quoniam suāvis est Dominus, in aeternum misericordia ejus, et usque in generātiōnem et generātiōnem vēritās ejus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{100}{Psalmus ipsī Dāvīd}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Misericordiam et jūdicium cantābō tibī Domine.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Psallem et intellegem in viā immaculātā, quandō veniēs ad mē. Perambulābam in innocentiā cordis meī, in mediō domūs meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Nōn prōpōnēbam ante oculōs meōs rem injūstam~; facientēs praevāricātiōnēs ōdīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Nōn adhaesit mihī cor prāvum~; dēclīnantem ā mē malignum nōn cognōscēbam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Dētrahentem sēcrētō proximō suō, hunc persequēbar~; superbō oculō, et insatiābilī corde, quum hōc nōn edēbam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Oculī meī ad fidēlēs terrae, ut sedeant mēcum~; ambulans in viā immaculātā, hic mihī ministrābat.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Nōn habitābit in mediō domūs meae quī facit superbiam~; quī loquitur inīqua nōn dīrexit in conspectū oculōrum meōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {In mātūtīnō interficiēbam omnēs peccātōrēs terrae, ut disperderem dē cīvitāte Dominī omnēs operantēs inīquitātem.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{14}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{101}{Ōrātiō pauperis quum anxius fuerit et in conspectū dominī effūderit precem suam}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Domine exaudī ōrātiōnem meam, et clāmor meus ad tē veniat.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Nōn āvertās faciem tuam ā mē. In quācumque diē trībulor, inclīnā ad mē aurem tuam~; in quācumque diē invocāverō tē, vēlōciter exaudī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quia dēfēcērunt sīcut fūmus diēs meī, et ossa mea sīcut cremium āruērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Percussus sum ut foenum, et āruit cor meum, quia oblītus sum comedere pānem meum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Ā vōce gemitūs meī adhaesit os meum carnī meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Similis factus sum pelicānō sōlitūdinis~; factus sum sīcut nicticorax in domiciliō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Vigilāvī, et factus sum sīcut passer sōlitārius in tectō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Tōtā diē exprobrābant mihī inimīcī meī, et quī laudābant mē adversum mē jūrābant~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {quia cinerem tamquam pānem mandūcābam, et pōtum meum cum flētū miscēbam,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {a faciē īrae et indignātiōnis tuae~; quia ēlevans allīsistī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Diēs meī sīcut umbrā dēclīnāvērunt, et egō sīcut foenum aruī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Tū autem, Domine, in aeternum permanēs, et memoriāle tuum in generātiōnem et generātiōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Tū exsurgens miserēberis Siōnis, quia tempus miserendī ejus, quia venit tempus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Quoniam placuērunt servīs tuīs lapidēs ejus, et terrae ejus miserēbuntur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Et timēbunt Gentēs nōmen tuum, Domine, et omnēs rēgēs terrae glōriam tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Quia aedificāvit Dominus Siōnem, et vidēbitur in glōriā suā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Respexit in ōrātiōnem humilium et nōn sprēvit precem eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Scrībantur haec in generātiōne alterā, et populus, quī creābitur, laudābit Dominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Quia prōspexit dē excelsō sanctō suō~; Dominus dē caelō in terram aspexit,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {ut audīret gemitūs compedītōrum~; ut solveret fīliōs interemptōrum~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {ut adnuntiet in Siōne nōmen Dominī, et laudem ejus in Jerosolimā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {In conveniendō populōs in ūnum, et rēgēs ut serviant Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Respondit eī in viā virtūtis suae, «~Paucitātem diērum meōrum nuntiā mihī.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Nē revocēs mē in dīmidiō diērum meōrum, in generātiōnem et generātiōnem annī tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Initiō tū, Domine, terram fundāvistī, et opera manuum tuārum sunt caelī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Ipsī perībunt, tū autem permanēs, et omnēs sīcut vestīmentum veterāscent, et sīcut opertōrium mūtābis eōs, et mūtābuntur~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {tū autem īdem ipse es, et annī tuī nōn dēficient.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Fīliī servōrum tuōrum habitābunt, et sēmen eōrum in saeculum dīrigētur.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{102}{Ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Benedīc, anima mea, Dominō, et omnia quae intrā mē sunt nōminī sanctō ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Benedīc, anima mea, Dominō, et nōlī oblīvīscī omnēs retribūtiōnēs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quī propitiātur omnibus inīquitātibus tuīs~; quī sānat omnēs infirmitātēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quī redimit dē interitū vītam tuam~; quī corōnat tē in misericordiā et miserātiōnibus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quī replet in bonīs dēsīderium tuum~; renovābitur ut aquilae juventūs tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Faciens misericordiās Dominus, et jūdicium omnibus injūriam patientibus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Nōtās fēcit viās suās Mōsī~; fīliīs Isrāēlis voluntātēs suās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Miserātor et misericors Dominus~; longanimis et multum misericors.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Nōn in perpetuum īrāscētur, neque in aeternum comminābitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Nōn secundum peccāta nostra fēcit nōbīs, neque secundum inīquitātēs nostrās retribuit nōbīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Quoniam secundum altitūdinem caelī ā terrā, corrōborāvit misericordiam suam super timentēs sē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Quantum distat ortus ab occidente, longē fēcit ā nōbīs inīquitātēs nostrās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Quōmodō miserētur pater fīliōrum, misertus est Dominus timentibus sē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Quoniam ipse cognōvit figmentum nostrum, recordātus est quoniam pulvis sumus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {homō, sīcut foenum diēs ejus, tamquam flōs agrī sīc efflōrēbit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Quoniam spīritus pertransīvit in illō, et nōn subsistet, et nōn cognōscet amplius locum suum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Misericordia autem Dominī ab aeternō et usque in aeternum super timentēs eum, et jūstitia illīus in fīliōs fīliōrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {hīs quī servant testāmentum ejus, et memorēs sunt mandātōrum ipsīus ad faciendum ea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Dominus in caelō parāvit sēdem suam, et regnum ipsīus omnibus dominābitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Benedīcite Dominō, omnēs angelī ejus~; potentēs virtūte, facientēs verbum illīus, ad audiendam vōcem sermōnum ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Benedīcite Dominō, omnēs virtūtēs ejus~; ministrī ejus, quī facitis voluntātem ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Benedīcite Dominō, omnia opera ejus~; in omnī locō dominātiōnis ejus, benedic, anima mea, Dominō.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{14}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{103}{Ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Benedic, anima mea, Dominō. Domine Deus meus, magnificātus es vehementer. Confessiōnem et decōrem induistī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {amictus lūmine sīcut vestīmentō, extendens caelum sīcut pellem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quī tegis aquīs superiōra ejus~; quī pōnis nūbem ascensum tuum~; quī ambulās super pennās ventōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quī facis angelōs tuōs spīritūs, et ministrōs tuōs ignem ūrentem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quī fundāvistī terram super stabilitātem suam~; nōn inclīnābitur in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Abissus sīcut vestīmentum amictus ejus~; super montēs stābunt aquae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ab increpātiōne tuā fugient~; ā vōce tonitruī tuī formīdābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Ascendunt montēs, et dēscendunt campī in locum quem fundāvistī eīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Terminum posuistī quem nōn transgredientur, neque convertentur operīre terram.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quī ēmittis fontēs in convallibus~; inter medium montium pertransībunt aquae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Pōtābunt omnēs bēstiae agrī~; expectābunt onagrī in sitī suā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Super ea volucrēs caelī habitābunt~; dē mediō petrārum dabunt vōcem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Rigans montēs dē superiōribus suīs~; dē fructū operum tuōrum satiābitur terra~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {prōdūcens foenum jūmentīs, et herbam servitūtī hominum, ut ēdūcās pānem dē terrā,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {et vīnum laetificet cor hominis, ut exhilaret faciem in oleō, et pānis cor hominis confirmet.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Saturābuntur ligna campī, et cedrī Libanī quās plantāvit~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {illīc passerēs nīdificābunt~; herodiī domus dux est eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Montēs excelsī cervīs~; petra refugium ērīnāceīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Fēcit lūnam in tempora~; sōl cognōvit occāsum suum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Posuistī tenebrās, et facta est nox~; in ipsā pertransībunt omnēs bēstiae silvae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {catulī leōnum rugientēs ut rapiant, et quaerant ā Deō ēscam sibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Ortus est sōl, et congregātī sunt, et in cubīlibus suīs collocābuntur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Exībit homō ad opus suum, et ad operātiōnem suam usque ad vesperum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Quam magnificāta sunt opera tua, Domine. Omnia in sapientiā fēcistī~; implēta est terra possessiōne tuā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Hoc mare magnum, et spatiōsum manibus~; illīc rēptilia quōrum nōn est numerus, animālia pusilla cum magnīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Illīc nāvēs pertransībunt~; dracō iste quem formāvistī ad illūdendum eī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Omnia ā tē expectant ut dēs illīs ēscam in tempore~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {dante tē illīs, colligent~; aperiente tē manum tuam, omnia implēbuntur bonitāte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Āvertente autem tē faciem, turbābuntur~; auferēs spīritum eōrum, et dēficient, et in pulverem suum revertentur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Ēmittēs Spīritum tuum, et creābuntur, et renovābis faciem terrae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Sit glōria Dominī in saeculum~; laetābitur Dominus in operibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}32}
  {Quī respicit terram, et facit eam tremere~; quī tangit montēs, et fūmigant.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}33}
  {Cantābō Dominō in vītā meā~; psallem Deō meō quamdiū sum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}34}
  {Jūcundum sit eī ēloquium meum~; egō vērō dēlectābor in Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}35}
  {Dēficiant peccātōrēs ā terrā, et inīquī, ita ut nōn sint. Benedic, anima mea, Dominō.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{14}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{104}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēminī Dominō, et invocāte nōmen ejus~; adnuntiāte inter gentēs opera ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Cantāte eī, et psallite eī~; narrāte omnia mīrābilia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Laudāminī in nōmine sanctō ejus~; laetētur cor quaerentium Dominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quaerite Dominum, et confirmāminī~; quaerite faciem ejus semper.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Mementōte mīrābilium ejus quae fēcit~; prōdigia ejus, et jūdicia ōris ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Sēmen Ābrahae, servī ejus~; fīliī Jācōbis, ēlectī ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ipse Dominus Deus noster~; in ūniversā terrā jūdicia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Memor fuit in saeculum testāmentī suī~; verbī quod mandāvit in mille generātiōnēs,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {quod disposuit ad Ābrahām, et jūrāmentī suī ad Isaac.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Et statūvit illud Jācōbī in praeceptum, et Isrāēlī in testāmentum aeternum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {dīcens, «~Tibī dabō terram Chanaan, fūniculum hērēditātis vestrae.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Quum essent numerō brevī, paucissimī, et incolae ejus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {et pertransīvērunt dē gente in gentem, et dē regnō ad populum alterum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Nōn relīquit hominem nocēre eīs, et corripuit prō eīs rēgēs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Nōlīte tangere chrīstōs meōs, et in profētīs meīs nōlīte malignārī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Et vocāvit famem super terram, et omne firmāmentum pānis contrīvit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Mīsit ante eōs virum~; in servum venundātus est Jōsēf.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Humiliāvērunt in compedibus pedēs ejus, ferrum pertransīvit animam ejus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {dōnec venīret verbum ejus~; ēloquium Dominī inflammāvit eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Mīsit rex et solvit eum, princeps populōrum, et dīmīsit eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Constitūvit eum dominum domūs suae, et principem omnis possessiōnis suae,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {ut ērudīret principēs ejus sīcut sēmet ipsum, et senēs ejus prūdentiam docēret.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Et intrāvit Isrāel in Aegiptum, et Jācōb accola fuit in terrā Chām.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Et auxit populum suum vehementer, et firmāvit eum super inimīcōs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Convertuit cor eōrum ut odīrent populum ejus, et dolum facerent in servōs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Mīsit Mōsem servum suum~; Aarōnem, quem ēlēgit ipsum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Posuit in eīs verba signōrum suōrum, et prōdigiōrum in terrā Chām.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {Mīsit tenebrās, et obscūrāvit, et nōn exacerbāvit sermōnēs suōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Convertuit aquās eōrum in sanguinem, et occīsit piscēs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Ēdidit terra eōrum rānās in  penetrālibus rēgum ipsōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Dixit, et vēnit cinomia et cinifēs in omnibus fīnibus eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}32}
  {Posuit pluviās eōrum in grandinem~; ignem combūrentem in terrā ipsōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}33}
  {Et percussit vīneās eōrum et fīculneās eōrum, et contrīvit lignum fīnium eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}34}
  {Dixit, et vēnit locusta, et brūchus cujus nōn erat numerus~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}35}
  {et comēdit omne foenum in terrā eōrum, et comēdit omnem fructum terrae eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}36}
  {Et percussit omne prīmōgenitum in terrā eōrum~; prīmitiās omnis labōris eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}37}
  {Et ēduxit eōs cum argentō et aurō, et nōn erat in tribūbus eōrum infirmus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}38}
  {Laetāta est Aegiptus in profectiōne eōrum, quia incubuit timor eōrum super eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}39}
  {Expandit nūbem in prōtectiōnem eōrum, et ignem ut lūcēret eīs per noctem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}40}
  {Petīvērunt, et vēnit coturnix, et pāne caelī saturāvit eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}41}
  {Dīrūpit petram, et fluxērunt aquae~; abīvērunt in siccō flūmina~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}42}
  {Quoniam memor fuit verbī sanctī suī, quod habuit ad Ābrahām puerum suum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}43}
  {Et ēduxit populum suum in exsultātiōne, et ēlectōs suōs in laetitiā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}44}
  {Et dedit illīs regiōnēs Gentium, et labōrēs populōrum possēdērunt~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}45}
  {ut custōdiant jūstificātiōnēs ejus, et lēgem ejus requīrant.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{15}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{105}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēminī Dominō quoniam bonus, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {¿~Quis loquētur potentiās Dominī, audītās faciet omnēs laudēs ejus~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Beātī quī custōdiunt jūdicium, et faciunt jūstitiam in omnī tempore.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Mementō nostrī, Domine, in benēplacitō populī tuī~; vīsitā nōs in salūtārī tuō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {ad videndum in bonitāte ēlectōrum tuōrum, ad laetandum in laetitiā gentis tuae, ut laudēris cum hērēditāte tuā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Peccāvimus cum patribus nostrīs~; injūstē ēgimus~; inīquitātem fēcimus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Patrēs nostrī in Aegiptō nōn intellexērunt mīrābilia tua~; nōn fuērunt memorēs multitūdinis misericordiae tuae, et irrītāvērunt ascendentēs in mare, mare Rubrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Et salvāvit eōs propter nōmen suum, ut nōtam faceret potentiam suam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Et increpuit mare Rubrum et exsiccātum est, et dēduxit eōs in abissīs sīcut in dēsertō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Et salvāvit eōs dē manū odientium, et redēmit eōs dē manū inimīcī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Et operuit aqua trībulantēs eōs~; ūnus ex eīs nōn remansit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Et crēdidērunt verbīs ejus, et laudāvērunt laudem ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Cito fēcērunt~; oblītī sunt operum ejus, et nōn sustinuērunt consilium ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Et concupīvērunt concupiscentiam in dēsertō, et tentāvērunt Deum in inaquōsō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Et dedit eīs petītiōnem ipsōrum, et mīsit saturitātem in animās eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Et irrītāvērunt Mōsem in castrīs~; Aarōnem, sanctum Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Aperta est terra, et dēgluttīvit Datanem, et operuit super congregātiōnem Abīrōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Et exarsit ignis in sinagōgā eōrum~; flamma combussit peccātōrēs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Et fēcērunt vitulum in Horeb, et adōrāvērunt sculptile.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Et mūtāvērunt glōriam suam in similitūdinem vitulī comedentis foenum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Oblītī sunt Deum quī salvāvit eōs~; quī fēcit magnālia in Aegiptō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {mīrābilia in terrā Cham, terribilia in marī Rubrō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Et dixit ut disperderet eōs, sī nōn Mōsēs ēlectus ejus stetisset in confractiōne in conspectū ejus, ut āverteret īram ejus nē disperderet eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Et prō nihilō habuērunt terram dēsīderābilem~; nōn crēdidērunt verbō ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Et murmurāvērunt in tabernāculīs suīs~; nōn exaudīvērunt vōcem Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Et ēlevāvit manum suam super eōs, ut prōsterneret eōs in dēsertō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Et ut dējiceret sēmen eōrum in Nātiōnibus, et dispergeret eōs in regiōnibus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {Et initiātī sunt Baalfegor, et comēdērunt sacrificia mortuōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Et irrītāvērunt eum in adinventiōnibus suīs, et multiplicāta est in eīs ruīna.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Et stetit Phinees et plācāvit, et cessāvit quassātiō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Et reputātum est eī in jūstitiam, in generātiōnem et generātiōnem usque in sempiternum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}32}
  {Et irrītāvērunt eum ad Aquās Contrādictiōnis, et vexātus est Mōsēs propter eōs,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}33}
  {quia exacerbāvērunt spīritum ejus, et distinxit in labiīs suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}34}
  {Nōn disperdidērunt gentēs quās dixit Dominus illīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}35}
  {Et commixtī sunt inter Gentēs, et didicērunt opera eōrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}36}
  {et servīvērunt sculptilibus eōrum, et factum est illīs in scandalum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}37}
  {Et immolāvērunt fīliōs suōs, et fīliās suās daemoniīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}38}
  {Et effūdērunt sanguinem innocentem, sanguinem fīliōrum suōrum et fīliārum suārum quās sacrificāvērunt sculptilibus Chanaānis, et infecta est terra in sanguinibus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}39}
  {Et contāmināta est in operibus eōrum, et fornicātī sunt in adinventiōnibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}40}
  {Et īrātus est furōre Dominus in populum suum, et abōminātus est hērēditātem suam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}41}
  {Et trādidit eōs in manūs gentium, et dominātī sunt eōrum quī ōdērunt eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}42}
  {Et trībulāvērunt eōs inimīcī eōrum, et humiliātī sunt sub manibus eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}43}
  {Saepe līberāvit eōs~; ipsī autem exacerbāvērunt eum in consiliō suō, et humiliātī sunt in inīquitātibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}44}
  {Et vīdit quum trībulārentur, et audīvit ōrātiōnem eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}45}
  {Et memor fuit testāmentī suī, et poenituit eum secundum multitūdinem misericordiae suae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}46}
  {Et dedit eōs in misericordiās in conspectū omnium quī cēperant eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}47}
  {Salvōs fac nōs, Domine Deus noster, et congregā nōs dē nātiōnibus, ut confiteāmur nōminī sanctō tuō, et glōriēmur in laude tuā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}48}
  {Benedictus Dominus Deus Isrāēlis, ā saeculō et usque in saeculum. Et dīcet omnis populus, «~Fīat, fīat.~»}


\psalmKathismaStasis{15}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{106}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēminī Dominō, quoniam bonus, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Dīcant quī redemptī sunt ā Dominō, quōs redēmit dē manū inimīcī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Dē regiōnibus congregāvit eōs, ā sōlis ortū et occāsū, et ab aquilōne et marī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Errāvērunt in sōlitūdine, in inaquōsō~; viam cīvitātis habitāculī nōn invēnērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Ēsurientēs et sitientēs~; anima eōrum in ipsīs dēfēcit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Et clāmāvērunt ad Dominum quum trībulārentur, et dē necessitātibus eōrum ēripuit eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Et dēduxit eōs in viam rectam, ut īrent in cīvitātem habitātiōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Confiteantur Dominō misericordiae ejus, et mīrābilia ejus fīliīs hominum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {quia satiāvit animam inānem, et animam ēsurientem satiāvit bonīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Sedentēs in tenebrīs et umbrā mortis~; vinctōs in mendīcitāte et ferrō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {quia exacerbāvērunt ēloquia Deī, et consilium Altissimī irrītāvērunt,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {et humiliātum est in labōribus cor eōrum~; infirmātī sunt, nec fuit quī adjuvāret.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Et clāmāvērunt ad Dominum quum trībulārentur, et dē necessitātibus eōrum līberāvit eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Et ēduxit eōs dē tenebrīs et umbrā mortis, et vincula eōrum dīrūpit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Confiteantur Dominō misericordiae ejus, et mīrābilia ejus fīliīs hominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Quia contrīvit portās aereās, et vectēs ferreōs confrēgit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Suscēpit eōs dē viā inīquitātis eōrum~; propter injūstitiās enim suās humiliātī sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Omnem ēscam abōmināta est anima eōrum, et appropinquāvērunt usque ad portās mortis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Et clāmāvērunt ad Dominum quum trībulārentur, et dē necessitātibus eōrum līberāvit eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Mīsit verbum suum, et sānāvit eōs, et ēripuit eōs dē interitiōnibus eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Confiteantur Dominō misericordiae ejus, et mīrābilia ejus fīliīs hominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Et sacrificent sacrificium laudis, et adnuntient opera ejus in exsultātiōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Quī dēscendunt mare in nāvibus, facientēs operātiōnem in aquīs multīs,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {ipsī vīdērunt opera Dominī, et mīrābilia ejus in prōfundō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Dixit, et stetit spīritus procellae, et exaltātī sunt fluctūs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Ascendunt usque ad caelōs, et dēscendunt usque ad abissōs~; anima eōrum in malīs tābēscēbat.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Turbātī sunt, et mōtī sunt sīcut ēbrius, et omnis sapientia eōrum dēvorāta est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {Et clāmāvērunt ad Dominum quum trībulārentur, et dē necessitātibus eōrum ēduxit eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Et statūvit procellam ejus in auram, et siluērunt fluctūs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Et laetātī sunt quia siluērunt, et dēduxit eōs in portum voluntātis eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Confiteantur Dominō misericordiae ejus, et mīrābilia ejus fīliīs hominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}32}
  {Exaltent eum in ecclēsiā plēbis, et in catēdrā seniōrum laudent eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}33}
  {Posuit flūmina in dēsertum et exitūs aquārum in sitim,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}34}
  {Terram fructiferam in salsūginem, ā malitiā inhabitantium in eā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}35}
  {Posuit dēsertum in stāgna aquārum, et terram sine aquā in exitūs aquārum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}36}
  {Et collocāvit illīc ēsurientēs, et constitūvērunt cīvitātem habitātiōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}37}
  {Et sēmināvērunt agrōs, et plantāvērunt vīneās, et fēcērunt fructum nātīvitātis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}38}
  {Et benedixit eīs, et multiplicātī sunt nimis, et jūmenta eōrum nōn minōrāvit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}39}
  {Et paucī factī sunt, et vexātī sunt ā trībulātiōne malōrum et dolōre.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}40}
  {Effūsa est contemptiō super principēs, et errāre fēcit eōs in inviō, et nōn in viā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}41}
  {Et adjūvit pauperem dē inopiā, et posuit sīcut ovēs familiās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}42}
  {Vidēbunt rectī, et laetābuntur, et omnis inīquitās oppīlābit ōs suum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}43}
  {¿~Quis sapiens, et custōdiet haec, et intelleget misericordiās Dominī~?}


\psalmKathismaStasis{15}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{107}{Canticum psalmī ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Parātum cor meum Deus, parātum cor meum~; cantābō, et psallem in glōriā meā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Exsurge, glōria mea~; exsurge, psaltērium et cittara~; exsurgem dīlūculō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Confitēbor tibī in populīs, Domine, et psallem tibī in nātiōnibus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {quia magna est super caelōs misericordia tua, et usque ad nūbēs vēritās tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Exaltāre super caelōs, Deus, et super omnem terram glōria tua,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {ut līberentur dīlectī tuī~; salvum fac dexterā tuā, et exaudī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Deus locūtus est in sanctō suō, «~Exsultābō, et dīvidem Sichimam, et convallem tabernāculōrum dīmētier.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Meus est Galād, et meus est Manassēs, et Efraim susceptiō capitis meī~; Jūda rex meus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Moāb lebēs speī meae~; in Idūmaeam extendem calceāmentum meum~; mihī aliēnigenae amīcī factī sunt.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {¿~Quis dēdūcet mē in cīvitātem mūnītam~? ¿~Quis dēdūcet mē usque in Idūmaeam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {¿~Nōnne tū, Deus, quī repulistī nōs~? ¿~Et nōn exībis, Deus, in virtūtibus nostrīs~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Dā nōbīs auxilium dē trībulātiōne, quia vāna salūs hominis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {In Deō faciēmus virtūtem, et ipse ad nihilum dēdūcet inimīcōs nostrōs.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{108}{In fīnem psalmus Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Deus, laudem meam nē tacuerīs, quia ōs peccātōris et ōs dolōsī super mē apertum est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Locūtī sunt adversum mē linguā dolōsā, et sermōnibus odiī circumdedērunt mē, et expugnāvērunt mē grātīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Prō eō ut mē dīligerent, dētrahēbant mihī~; egō autem ōrābam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Et posuērunt adversum mē mala prō bonīs, et odium prō dīlectiōne meā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Constitue super eum peccātōrem, et diabolus stet ā dextrīs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Quum jūdicātur, exiat condemnātus, et ōrātiō ejus fīat in peccātum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Fīant diēs ejus paucī, et epīscopātum ejus accipiat alter.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Fīant fīliī ejus orfanī, et uxor ejus vidua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Nūtantēs transferantur fīliī ejus et mendīcent, et ējiciantur dē habitātiōnibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Scrūtētur foenerātor omnem substantiam ejus, et dīripiant aliēnī labōrēs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Nōn sit illī adjūtor, nec sit quī misereātur pūpillīs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Fīant nātī ejus in interitum~; in generātiōne ūnā dēleātur nōmen ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {In memoriam rediat inīquitās patrum ejus in conspectū Dominī, et peccātum mātris ejus nōn dēleātur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Fīant contrā Dominum semper, et dispereat dē terrā memoria eōrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {prō eō quod nōn est recordātus facere misericordiam, et persecūtus est hominem inopem et mendīcum, et compunctum corde, mortificāre.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Et dīlexit maledictiōnem, et veniet eī. Et nōluit benedictiōnem, et ēlongābitur ab eō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Et indūvit maledictiōnem sīcut vestīmentum, et intrāvit sīcut aqua in interiōra ejus, et sīcut oleum in ossibus ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Fīat eī sīcut vestīmentum, quō operītur, et sīcut zōna quā semper praecingitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Hoc opus eōrum quī dētrahunt mihī apud Dominum, et quī loquuntur mala adversus animam meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Et tū, Domine, Domine, fac mēcum propter nōmen tuum, quia suāvis est misericordia tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Līberā mē, quia egēnus et pauper egō sum, et cor meum conturbātum est intrā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Sīcut umbra quum dēclīnat ablātus sum, et excussus sum sīcut locustae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Genua mea infirmāta sunt ā jējūniō, et carō mea immūtāta est propter oleum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Et egō factus sum opprobrium illīs~; vīdērunt mē, et mōvērunt capita sua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Adjuvā mē, Domine Deus meus~; salvum mē fac secundum misericordiam tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Et sciant quia manus tua haec, et tū, Domine, fēcistī eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {Maledīcent illī, et tū benedīcēs~; quī insurgunt in mē, confundantur, servus autem tuus laetābitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Induantur quī dētrahunt mihī pudōre, et operiantur sīcut diploide confūsiōne suā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Confitēbor Dominō nimis in ōre meō, et in mediō multōrum laudābō eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Quia astitit ā dextrīs pauperis, ut salvam faceret ā persequentibus animam meam.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{16}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{109}{Psalmus Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Dixit Dominus Dominō meō, «~Sedē ā dextrīs meīs, dōnec pōnam inimīcōs tuōs scabellum pedum tuōrum.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Virgam virtūtis tuae ēmittet Dominus ex Siōne~; domināre in mediō inimīcōrum tuōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Tēcum principium in diē virtūtis tuae, in splendōribus sanctōrum~; ex uterō ante lūciferum genuī tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Jūrāvit Dominus et nōn poenitēbit eum, «~Tū es sacerdōs in aeternum secundum ordinem Melchisedech.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Dominus ā dextrīs tuīs~; confrēgit in diē īrae suae rēgēs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Jūdicābit in nātiōnibus, implēbit ruīnās~; conquassābit capita in terrā multōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Dē torrente in viā bibet~; proptereā exaltābit caput.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{110}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēbor tibī, Domine, in tōtō corde meō~; in consiliō jūstōrum et congregātiōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Magna opera Dominī, exquīsīta in omnēs voluntātēs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Confessiō et magnificentia opus ejus, et jūstitia ejus manet in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Memoriam fēcit mīrābilium suōrum~; misericors et miserātor Dominus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Ēscam dedit timentibus sē. Memor erit in saeculum testāmentī suī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Virtūtem operum suōrum adnuntiābit populō suō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {ut det illīs hērēditātem gentium~; opera manuum ejus vēritās et jūdicium.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Fidēlia omnia mandāta ejus, confirmāta in saeculum saeculī, facta in vēritāte et aequitāte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Redemptiōnem mīsit populō suō~; mandāvit in aeternum testāmentum suum. sanctum, et terribile nōmen ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Initium sapientiae timor Dominī~; intellectus bonus omnibus facientibus eum. Laudātiō ejus manet in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{111}{Allēlūia reversiōnis Aggaeī et Zacharīae}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Beātus vir, quī timet Dominum~; in mandātīs ejus volet nimis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Potens in terrā erit sēmen ejus~; generātiō rectōrum benedīcētur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Glōria et dīvitiae in domū ejus, et jūstitia ejus manet in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Exortum est in tenebrīs lūmen rectīs~; misericors, et miserātor, et jūstus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Jūcundus homō quī miserētur et commodat~; dispōnet sermōnēs suōs in jūdiciō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {quia in aeternum nōn commovēbitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {In memoriā aeternā erit jūstus~; ab audītiōne malā nōn timēbit~; parātum cor ejus spērāre in Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Confirmātum est cor ejus~; nōn commovēbitur dōnec dēspiciat inimīcōs suōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Dispersit~; dēdit pauperibus~; jūstitia ejus manet in saeculum saeculī~; cornū ejus exaltābitur in glōriā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Peccātor vidēbit, et īrāscētur~; dentibus suīs fremet et tābēscet~; dēsīderium peccātōrum perībit.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{16}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{112}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudāte, puerī, Dominum~; laudāte nōmen Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Sit nōmen Dominī benedictum, ex hōc nunc, et usque in saeculum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Ā sōlis ortū usque ad occāsum laudābile nōmen Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Excelsus super omnēs gentēs Dominus, et super caelōs glōria ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {¿~Quis sīcut Dominus Deus noster, quī in altīs habitat,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {et humilia respicit in caelō et in terrā~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Suscitans ā terrā inopem, et dē stercore ērigens pauperem,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Ut collocet eum cum principibus, cum principibus populī suī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Quī habitāre facit sterilem in domū, mātrem fīliōrum laetantem.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{113}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {In exitū Isrāel dē Aegiptō, domus Jācōb dē populō barbarō,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {facta est Jūdaea sanctificātiō ejus~; Isrāel potestās ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Mare vīdit et fūgit~; Jordānis conversus est retrorsum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Montēs exsultāvērunt ut arietēs, et collēs sīcut agnī ovium.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {¿~Quid est tibī, mare, quod fūgistī~? ¿~Et tū, Jordānis, quia conversus es retrorsum~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Montēs, ¿~exsultāvistis sīcut arietēs~? Et collēs, ¿~sīcut agnī ovium~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ā faciē Dominī mōta est terra, ā faciē Deī Jācōbis,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {quī convertuit petram in stāgna aquārum, et rūpem in fontēs aquārum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Nōn nōbīs, Domine, nōn nōbīs, sed nōminī tuō dā glōriam, super misericordiā tuā et vēritāte tuā,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {nēquandō dīcant Gentēs, «~¿~Ubi est Deus eōrum~?~».}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Deus autem noster in caelō~; omnia quaecumque voluit fēcit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Simulācra gentium argentum et aurum, opera manuum hominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Ōs habent, et nōn loquentur~; oculōs habent, et nōn vidēbunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Aurēs habent, et nōn audient~; nārēs habent, et nōn odōrābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Manūs habent, et nōn palpābunt~; pedēs habent, et nōn ambulābunt~; nōn clāmābunt in gutture suō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Similēs illīs fīant quī faciunt ea, et omnēs quī confīdunt in eīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Domus Isrāēlis spērāvit in Dominō~; adjūtor eōrum et prōtector eōrum est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Domus Aarōnis spērāvit in Dominō~; adjūtor eōrum et prōtector eōrum est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Quī timent Dominum, spērāvērunt in Dominō~; adjūtor eōrum et prōtector eōrum est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Dominus memor fuit nostrī, et benedixit nōbīs. Benedixit domuī Isrāēlis~; benedixit domuī Aarōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {benedixit omnibus quī timent Dominum, pusillīs cum majōribus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Adiciat Dominus super vōs~; super vōs et super fīliōs vestrōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Benedictī vōs ā Dominō, quī fēcit caelum et terram.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Caelum caelī Dominō~; terram autem dedit fīliīs hominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Nōn mortuī laudābunt tē, Domine, neque omnēs quī dēscendunt in infernum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Sed nōs quī vīvimus benedīcimus Dominō, ex hōc nunc et usque in saeculum.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{114}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Dīlexī, quoniam exaudiet Dominus vōcem ōrātiōnis meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Quia inclīnāvit aurem suam mihī, et in diēbus meīs invocābō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Circumdedērunt mē dolōrēs mortis, et perīcula infernī invēnērunt mē~; trībulātiōnem et dolōrem invēnī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {et nōmen Dominī invocāvī~; Ō Domine, līberā animam meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Misericors Dominus, et jūstus, et Deus noster miserētur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Custōdiens parvulōs Dominus~; humiliātus sum, et līberāvit mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Convertere, anima mea, in requiem tuam, quia Dominus benefēcit tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Quia ēripuit animam meam dē morte, oculōs meōs ā lacrimīs, pedēs meōs ā lāpsū.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Placēbō Dominō in regiōne vīvōrum.}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{115}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Crēdidī, propter quod locūtus sum~; egō autem humiliātus sum nimis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Egō dixī in excessū meō, «~Omnis homō mendax.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {¿~Quid retribuem Dominō, prō omnibus, quae retribuit mihī~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Calicem salūtāris accipiem, et nōmen Dominī invocābō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Vōta mea Dominō reddem cōram omnī populō ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Pretiōsa in conspectū Dominī mors sanctōrum ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ō Domine, quia egō servus tuus~; egō servus tuus, et fīlius ancillae tuae~; dīrūpistī vincula mea.}

  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Tibī sacrificābō hostiam laudis, et nōmen Dominī invocābō.}

\psalmVerse

\psalmChapterWithInscription{116}{Allēlūia}
