\psalmChapterWithInscription{117}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēminī Dominō, quoniam bonus, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Dīcat nunc Isrāel quoniam bonus, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Dīcat nunc domus Aarōnis, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Dīcant nunc quī timent Dominum, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Dē trībulātiōne invocāvī Dominum, et exaudīvit mē in lātitūdinem Dominus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Dominus mihī adjūtor~; nōn timēbō quid faciat mihī homō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Dominus mihī adjūtor, et egō dēspiciam inimīcōs meōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Bonum est confīdere in Dominō, quam confīdere in homine.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Bonum est spērāre in Dominō, quam spērāre in principibus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Omnēs gentēs circumīvērunt mē, et in nōmine Dominī quia ultus sum in eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Circumdantēs circumdedērunt mē, et in nōmine Dominī quia ultus sum in eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Circumdedērunt mē sīcut apēs, et exarsērunt sīcut ignis in spīnīs, et in nōmine Dominī quia ultus sum in eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Impulsus ēversus sum ut caderem, et Dominus suscēpit mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Fortitūdō mea et laus mea Dominus, et factus est mihī in salūtem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Vox exsultātiōnis et salūtis in tabernāculīs jūstōrum. Dextera Dominī fēcit virtūtem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Dextera Dominī exaltāvit mē~; dextera Dominī fēcit virtūtem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Nōn morier, sed vīvem, et narrābō opera Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Castīgans castīgāvit mē Dominus, et mortī nōn trādidit mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Aperīte mihī portās jūstitiae~; ingressus in eās confitēbor Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Haec porta Dominī~; jūstī intrābunt in eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Confitēbor tibī quoniam exaudīvistī mē, et factus es mihī in salūtem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Lapidem quem reprobāvērunt aedificantēs, hic factus est in caput angulī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Ā Dominō factum est istud, et est mīrābile in oculīs nostrīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Haec est diēs quam fēcit Dominus~; exsultēmus, et laetēmur in eā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Ō Domine, salvum mē fac. Ō Domine, bene prōsperāre.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}

\psalmVerse

\psalmVerse

  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Confitēminī Dominō, quoniam bonus, quoniam in saeculum misericordia ejus.}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{118}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Beātī immaculātī in viā, quī ambulant in lēge Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Beātī, quī scrūtantur testimōnia ejus~; in tōtō corde exquīrent eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Nōn enim quī operantur inīquitātem in viīs ejus ambulāvērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Tū mandāvistī mandāta tua custōdīrī nimis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Utinam dīrigantur viae meae ad custōdiendās jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Tunc nōn confundar, quum perspexerō in omnibus mandātīs tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Confitēbor tibī in dīrectiōne cordis, in eō quod didicī jūdicia jūstitiae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Jūstificātiōnēs tuās custōdiem~; nōn mē dērelinquās usquequāque.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {¿~In quō corrigit adolēscentior viam suam~? In custōdiendō sermōnēs tuōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {In tōtō corde meō exquīsīvī tē~; nē repellās mē ā mandātīs tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {In corde meō abscondī ēloquia tua, ut nōn peccem tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Benedictus es Domine~; docē mē jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {In labiīs meīs prōnuntiāvī omnia jūdicia ōris tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {In viā testimōniōrum tuōrum dēlectātus sum, sīcut in omnibus dīvitiīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {In mandātīs tuīs exercēbor, et consīderābō viās tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {In jūstificātiōnibus tuīs meditābor~; nōn oblīvīscer sermōnēs tuōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Retribue servō tuō~; vīvificā mē, et custōdiem sermōnēs tuōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Revēlā oculōs meōs, et consīderābō mīrābilia dē lēge tuā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Incola egō sum in terrā~; nōn abscondās ā mē mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Concupīvit anima mea dēsīderāre jūstificātiōnēs tuās in omnī tempore.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Increpāvistī superbōs~; maledictī quī dēclīnant ā mandātīs tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Aufer ā mē opprobrium, et contemptum, quia testimōnia tua exquīsīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Etenim sēdērunt principēs, et adversum mē loquēbantur~; servus autem tuus exercēbātur in jūstificātiōnibus tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Nam et testimōnia tua meditātiō mea est, et consilium meum jūstificātiōnēs tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}25}
  {Adhaesit pavīmentō anima mea~; vīvificā mē secundum verbum tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}26}
  {Viās meās ēnuntiāvī, et exaudīvistī mē~; docē mē jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Viam jūstificātiōnum tuārum instrue mē, et exercēbor in mīrābilibus tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}28}
  {Dormītāvit anima mea prae taediō~; confirmā mē in verbīs tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}29}
  {Viam inīquitātis āmovē ā mē, et dē lēge tuā miserēre meī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}30}
  {Viam vēritātis ēlēgī~; jūdicia tua nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}31}
  {Adhaesī testimōniīs tuīs, Domine~; nōlī mē confundere.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}32}
  {Viam mandātōrum tuōrum cucurrī, quum dīlātāvistī cor meum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}33}
  {Lēgem pōne mihī, Domine, viam jūstificātiōnum tuārum, et exquīram eam semper.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}34}
  {Dā mihī intellectum, et scrūtābor lēgem tuam, et custōdiem illam in tōtō corde meō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}35}
  {Dēdūc mē in sēmitam mandātōrum tuōrum, quia ipsam voluī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}36}
  {Inclīnā cor meum in testimōnia tua, et nōn in avāritiam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}37}
  {Āverte oculōs meōs nē videant vānitātem~; in viā tuā vīvificā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}38}
  {Statue servō tuō ēloquium tuum in timōre tuō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}39}
  {Amputā opprobrium meum quod suspicātus sum, quia jūdicia tua jūcunda.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}40}
  {Ecce concupīvī mandāta tua~; in aequitāte tuā vīvificā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}41}
  {Et veniat super mē misericordia tua, Domine~; salūtāre tuum secundum ēloquium tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}42}
  {Et respondēbō exprobrantibus mihī verbum, quia spērāvī in sermōnibus tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}43}
  {Et nē auferās dē ōre meō verbum vēritātis usquequāque, quia in jūdiciīs tuīs superspērāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}44}
  {Et custōdiem lēgem tuam semper, in saeculum et in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}45}
  {Et ambulābam in lātitūdine, quia mandāta tua exquīsīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}46}
  {Et loquēbar in testimōniīs tuīs in conspectū rēgum, et nōn confundēbar.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}47}
  {Et meditābar in mandātīs tuīs, quae dīlexī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}48}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}49}
  {Memor estō verbī tuī servō tuō, in quō mihī spem dedistī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}50}
  {Haec mē consōlāta est in humilitāte meā, quia ēloquium tuum vīvificāvit mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}51}
  {Superbī inīquē agēbant usquequāque, ā lēge autem tua nōn dēclīnāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}52}
  {Memor fuī jūdiciōrum tuōrum ā saeculō Domine, et consōlātus sum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}53}
  {Dēfectiō tenuit mē, prō peccātōribus dērelinquentibus lēgem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}54}
  {Cantābilēs mihī erant jūstificātiōnēs tuae in locō peregrīnātiōnis meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}55}
  {Memor fuī nocte nōminis tuī Domine, et custōdīvī lēgem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}56}
  {Haec facta est mihī, quia jūstificātiōnēs tuās exquīsīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}57}
  {Portiō mea, Domine~; dixī custōdīre lēgem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}58}
  {Dēprecātus sum faciem tuam in tōtō corde meō~; miserēre meī secundum ēloquium tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}59}
  {Cōgitāvī viās meās, et convertuī pedēs meōs in testimōnia tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}60}
  {Parātus sum, et nōn sum turbātus, ut custōdiam mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}61}
  {Fūnēs peccātōrum circumplexī sunt mē, et lēgem tuam nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}62}
  {Mediā nocte surgēbam, ad confitendum tibī super jūdicia jūstificātiōnis tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}63}
  {Particeps egō sum omnium timentium tē, et custōdientium mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}64}
  {Misericordia tua, Domine, plēna est terra~; jūstificātiōnēs tuās docē mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}65}
  {Bonitātem fēcistī cum servō tuō, Domine, secundum verbum tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}66}
  {Bonitātem et disciplīnam et scientiam docē mē, quia mandātīs tuīs crēdidī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}67}
  {Priusquam humiliārer egō dēlīquī~; proptereā ēloquium tuum custōdīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}68}
  {Bonus es tū, et in bonitāte tuā docē mē jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}69}
  {Multiplicāta est super mē inīquitās superbōrum~; egō autem in tōtō corde meō scrūtābor mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}70}
  {Coāgulātum est sīcut lac cor eōrum~; egō vērō lēgem tuam meditātus sum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}71}
  {Bonum mihī quia humiliāvistī mē, ut discam jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}72}
  {Bonum mihī lex ōris tuī, super millia aurī et argentī.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{17}{2}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}73}
  {Manūs tuae fēcērunt mē, et plasmāvērunt mē~; dā mihī intellectum, et discam mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}74}
  {Quī timent tē vidēbunt mē, et laetābuntur, quia in verba tua superspērāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}75}
  {Cognōvī, Domine, quia aequitās jūdicia tua, et in vēritāte tuā humiliāvistī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}76}
  {Fīat misericordia tua ut consōlētur mē, secundum ēloquium tuum servō tuō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}77}
  {Veniant mihī miserātiōnēs tuae, et vīvam, quia lex tua meditātiō mea est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}78}
  {Confundantur superbī, quia injūstē inīquitātem fēcērunt in mē~; egō autem exercēbor in mandātīs tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}79}
  {Convertantur mihī timentēs tē, et quī nōvērunt testimōnia tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}80}
  {Fīat cor meum immaculātum in jūstificātiōnibus tuīs, ut nōn confundar.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}81}
  {Dēfēcit in salūtāre tuum anima mea, et in verbum tuum superspērāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}82}
  {Dēfēcērunt oculī meī in ēloquium tuum, dīcentēs, «~¿~Quandō consōlāberis mē~?~».}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}83}
  {Quia factus sum sīcut uter in pruīnā~; jūstificātiōnēs tuās nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}84}
  {¿~Quot sunt diēs servī tuī~? ¿~Quandō faciēs dē persequentibus mē jūdicium~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}85}
  {Narrāvērunt mihī inīquī fābulātiōnēs, sed nōn ut lex tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}86}
  {Omnia mandāta tua vēritās~; inīquē persecūtī sunt mē~; adjuvā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}87}
  {Paulō minus consummāvērunt mē in terrā~; egō autem nōn dērelīquī mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}88}
  {Secundum misericordiam tuam vīvificā mē, et custōdiem testimōnia ōris tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}89}
  {In aeternum, Domine, verbum tuum permanet in caelō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}90}
  {In generātiōnem et generātiōnem vēritās tua~; fundāvistī terram, et permanet.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}91}
  {Ordinātiōne tuā persevērat diēs, quoniam omnia serviunt tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}92}
  {Nisī quod lex tua meditātiō mea est, tunc forte perīvissem in humilitāte meā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}93}
  {In aeternum nōn oblīvīscer jūstificātiōnēs tuās, quia in ipsīs vīvificāvistī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}94}
  {Tuus sum egō~; salvum mē fac, quoniam jūstificātiōnēs tuās exquīsīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}95}
  {Mē expectāvērunt peccātōrēs ut perderent mē~; testimōnia tua intellexī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}96}
  {Omnis consummātiōnis vīdī fīnem, lātum mandātum tuum nimis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}97}
  {Quōmodō dīlexī lēgem tuam, Domine~; tōtā diē meditātiō mea est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}98}
  {Super inimīcōs meōs prūdentem mē fēcistī mandātō tuō, quia in aeternum mihī est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}99}
  {Super omnēs docentēs mē intellexī, quia testimōnia tua meditātiō mea est.}


\psalmVerse
  {100}
  {Super senēs intellexī, quia mandāta tua quaesīvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {101}
  {Ab omnī viā malā prohibuī pedēs meōs, ut custōdiam verba tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {102}
  {Ā jūdiciīs tuīs nōn dēclīnāvī, quia tū lēgem posuistī mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {103}
  {Quam dulcia faucibus meīs ēloquia tua, super mel ōrī meō.}


\psalmVerse
  {104}
  {Ā mandātīs tuīs intellexī~; proptereā ōdīvī omnem viam inīquitātis.}


\psalmVerse
  {105}
  {Lucerna pedibus meīs verbum tuum, et lūmen sēmitīs meīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {106}
  {Jūrāvī et statūvī custōdīre jūdicia jūstitiae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {107}
  {Humiliātus sum usquequāque, Domine~; vīvificā mē secundum verbum tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {108}
  {Voluntāria ōris meī benēplacita fac, Domine, et jūdicia tua docē mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {109}
  {Anima mea in manibus meīs semper, et lēgem tuam nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmVerse
  {110}
  {Posuērunt peccātōrēs laqueum mihī, et dē mandātīs tuīs nōn errāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {111}
  {Hērēditāte acquīsīvī testimōnia tua in aeternum, quia exsultātiō cordis meī sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {112}
  {Inclīnāvī cor meum ad faciendās jūstificātiōnēs tuās in aeternum, propter retribūtiōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {113}
  {Inīquōs odiō habuī, et lēgem tuam dīlexī.}


\psalmVerse
  {114}
  {Adjūtor et susceptor meus es tū, et in verbum tuum superspērāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {115}
  {Dēclīnāte ā mē, malignī, et scrūtābor mandāta Deī meī.}


\psalmVerse
  {116}
  {Suscipe mē secundum ēloquium tuum, et vīvam, et nōn confundās mē ab expectātiōne meā.}


\psalmVerse
  {117}
  {Adjuvā mē, et salvus erō, et meditābor in jūstificātiōnibus tuīs semper.}


\psalmVerse
  {118}
  {Sprēvistī omnēs discēdentēs ā jūdiciīs tuīs, quia injūsta cōgitātiō eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {119}
  {Praevāricantēs reputāvī omnēs peccātōrēs terrae~; ideō dīlexī testimōnia tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {120}
  {Confīge timōre tuō carnēs meās~; ā jūdiciīs enim tuīs timuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {121}
  {Fēcī jūdicium et jūstitiam~; nōn trādās mē calumniantibus mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {122}
  {Suscipe servum tuum in bonum~; nōn calumnientur mē superbī.}


\psalmVerse
  {123}
  {Oculī meī dēfēcērunt in salūtāre tuum, et in ēloquium jūstitiae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {124}
  {Fac cum servō tuō secundum misericordiam tuam, et jūstificātiōnēs tuās docē mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {125}
  {Servus tuus sum egō~; dā mihī intellectum, ut sciam testimōnia tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {126}
  {Tempus faciendī, Domine~; dissipāvērunt lēgem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {127}
  {Ideō dīlexī mandāta tua super aurum et topāzion.}


\psalmVerse
  {128}
  {Proptereā ad omnia mandāta tua dīrigēbar~; omnem viam inīquam odiō habuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {129}
  {Mīrābilia testimōnia tua~; ideō scrūtāta est ea anima mea.}


\psalmVerse
  {130}
  {Dēclārātiō sermōnum tuōrum illūminat, et intellectum dat parvulīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {131}
  {Ōs meum aperuī, et attraxī spīritum, quia mandāta tua dēsīderābam.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{17}{3}

\psalmVerse
  {132}
  {Aspice in mē, et miserēre meī, secundum jūdicium dīligentium nōmen tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {133}
  {Gressūs meōs dīrige secundum ēloquium tuum, et nōn dominētur meī omnis injūstitia.}


\psalmVerse
  {134}
  {Redime mē ā calumniīs hominum, ut custōdiam mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {135}
  {Faciem tuam illūminā super servum tuum, et docē mē jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {136}
  {Exitūs aquārum dēduxērunt oculī meī, quia nōn custōdīvērunt lēgem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {137}
  {Jūstus es Domine, et rectum jūdicium tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {138}
  {Mandāvistī jūstitiam testimōnia tua, et vēritātem tuam nimis.}


\psalmVerse
  {139}
  {Tābēscere mē fēcit zēlus meus, quia oblītī sunt verba tua inimīcī meī.}


\psalmVerse
  {140}
  {Ignītum ēloquium tuum vehementer, et servus tuus dīlexit illud.}


\psalmVerse
  {141}
  {Adolēscentulus sum egō et contemptus~; jūstificātiōnēs tuās nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmVerse
  {142}
  {Jūstitia tua jūstitia in aeternum, et lex tua vēritās.}


\psalmVerse
  {143}
  {Trībulātiō et angustia invēnērunt mē~; mandāta tua meditātiō mea est.}


\psalmVerse
  {144}
  {Aequitās testimōnia tua in aeternum~; intellectum dā mihī, et vīvam.}


\psalmVerse
  {145}
  {Clāmāvī in tōtō corde meō, exaudī mē, Domine~; jūstificātiōnēs tuās requīrem.}


\psalmVerse
  {146}
  {Clāmāvī ad tē~; salvum mē fac, ut custōdiam mandāta tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {147}
  {Praevēnī in mātūritāte, et clāmāvī, quia in verba tua superspērāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {148}
  {Praevēnērunt oculī meī ad tē dīlūculō, ut meditārer ēloquia tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {149}
  {Vōcem meam audī secundum misericordiam tuam Domine, et secundum jūdicium tuum vīvificā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {150}
  {Appropinquāvērunt persequentēs mē inīquitātī, ā lēge autem tuā longē factī sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {151}
  {Prope es tū Domine, et omnēs viae tuae vēritās.}


\psalmVerse
  {152}
  {Initiō cognōvī dē testimōniīs tuīs, quia in aeternum fundāvistī ea.}


\psalmVerse
  {153}
  {Vidē humilitātem meam, et ēripe mē, quia lēgem tuam nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmVerse
  {154}
  {Jūdicā jūdicium meum, et redime mē~; propter ēloquium tuum vīvificā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {155}
  {Longē ā peccātōribus salūs, quia jūstificātiōnēs tuās nōn exquīsīvērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {156}
  {Misericordiae tuae multae, Domine~; secundum jūdicium tuum vīvificā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {157}
  {Multī quī persequuntur mē, et trībulant mē~; ā testimōniīs tuīs nōn dēclīnāvī.}


\psalmVerse
  {158}
  {Vīdī praevāricantēs et tābēscēbam, quia ēloquia tua nōn custōdīvērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {159}
  {Vidē quoniam mandāta tua dīlexī, Domine~; in misericordiā tuā vīvificā mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {160}
  {principium verbōrum tuōrum vēritās~; in aeternum omnia jūdicia jūstitiae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {161}
  {principēs persecūtī sunt mē grātīs, et ā verbīs tuīs formīdāvit cor meum.}


\psalmVerse
  {162}
  {Laetābor egō super ēloquia tua, sīcut quī invēnit spolia multa.}


\psalmVerse
  {163}
  {Inīquitātem odiō habuī, et abōminātus sum~; lēgem autem tuam dīlexī.}


\psalmVerse
  {164}
  {Septiēs in diē laudem dixī tibī, super jūdicia jūstitiae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {165}
  {Pax multa dīligentibus lēgem tuam, et nōn est illīs scandalum.}


\psalmVerse
  {166}
  {Expectābam salūtāre tuum, Domine, et mandāta tua dīlexī.}


\psalmVerse
  {167}
  {Custōdīvit anima mea testimōnia tua, et dīlexit ea vehementer.}


\psalmVerse
  {168}
  {Servāvī mandāta tua et testimōnia tua, quia omnēs viae meae in conspectū tuō.}


\psalmVerse
  {169}
  {Appropinquet dēprecātiō mea in conspectū tuō, Domine~; juxtā ēloquium tuum dā mihī intellectum.}


\psalmVerse
  {170}
  {Intret postulātiō mea in conspectū tuō~; secundum ēloquium tuum ēripe mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {171}
  {Ēructābunt labia mea himnum, quum docuerīs mē jūstificātiōnēs tuās.}


\psalmVerse
  {172}
  {Prōnuntiābit lingua mea ēloquium tuum, quia omnia mandāta tua aequitās.}


\psalmVerse
  {173}
  {Fīat manus tua ut salvet mē, quoniam mandāta tua ēlēgī.}


\psalmVerse
  {174}
  {Concupīvī salūtāre tuum, Domine, et lex tua meditātiō mea est.}


\psalmVerse
  {175}
  {Vīvet anima mea, et laudābit tē, et jūdicia tua adjuvābunt mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {176}
  {Errāvī sīcut ovis quae perīvit~; quaere servum tuum, quia mandāta tua nōn sum oblītus.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{18}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{119}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Ad Dominum quum trībulārer clāmāvī, et exaudīvit mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Domine, līberā animam meam ā labiīs inīquīs et ā linguā dolōsā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {¿~Quid dētur tibī, aut quid appōnātur tibī ad linguam dolōsam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Sagittae potentis acūtae, cum carbōnibus dēsōlātōriīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Heu mihī, quia incolātus meus prolongātus est. Habitāvī cum habitantibus Cēdar~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {multum incola fuit anima mea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Cum hīs quī ōdērunt pācem, eram pācificus~; quum loquēbar illīs, impugnābant mē grātīs.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{120}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Levāvī oculōs meōs in montēs, unde veniet auxilium mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Auxilium meum ā Dominō, quī fēcit caelum et terram.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Nōn det in commōtiōnem pedem tuum, neque dormītet quī custōdit tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Ecce nōn dormītābit neque dormiet quī custōdit Isrāēlem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Dominus custōdit tē, Dominus prōtectiō tua super manum dexteram tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Per diem sōl nōn ūret tē, neque lūna per noctem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Dominus custōdit tē ab omnī malō~; custōdiat animam tuam Dominus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Dominus custōdiat introitum tuum, et exitum tuum, ex hōc nunc, et usque in saeculum.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{121}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laetātus sum in hīs quae dicta sunt mihī, «~In domum Dominī ībimus.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Stantēs erant pedēs nostrī in ātriīs tuīs, Jerosolima.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Jerosolima, quae aedificātur ut cīvitās, cujus participātiō ejus in idipsum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Illūc enim ascensērunt tribūs, tribūs Dominī, testimōnium Isrāēlis, ad confitendum nōminī Dominī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quia illīc sēdērunt sēdēs in jūdiciō, sēdēs super domum Dāvid.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Rogāte quae ad pācem sunt Jerosolimae, et abundantiā dīligentibus tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Fīat pax in virtūte tuā, et abundantia in turribus tuīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Propter frātrēs meōs et proximōs meōs, loquēbar pācem dē tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Propter domum Dominī Deī nostrī, quaesīvī bona tibī.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{122}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Ad tē levāvī oculōs meōs, quī habitās in caelīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Ecce sīcut oculī servōrum in manibus dominōrum suōrum~; sīcut oculī ancillae in manibus dominae suae, ita oculī nostrī ad Dominum Deum nostrum, dōnec misereātur nostrī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Miserēre nostrī, Domine, miserēre nostrī, quia multum replētī sumus dēspectiōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quia multum replēta est anima nostra~; opprobrium abundantibus, et dēspectiō superbīs.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{123}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Nisī quia Dominus erat in nōbīs, dīcat nunc Isrāel,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {nisī quia Dominus erat in nōbīs, quum exsurgērent hominēs in nōs,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {forte vīvōs dēgluttīvissent nōs, quum īrāscerētur furor eōrum in nōs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {forsitan aqua absorbuisset nōs~; torrentem pertransīvit anima nostra~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {forsitan pertransīvisset anima nostra aquam intolerābilem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Benedictus Dominus, quī nōn dedit nōs, in captiōnem dentibus eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Anima nostra sīcut passer ērepta est dē laqueō vēnantium~; laqueus contrītus est, et nōs līberātī sumus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Adjūtōrium nostrum in nōmine Dominī, quī fēcit caelum et terram.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{18}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{124}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Quī confīdunt in Dominō, sīcut mons Siōnis~; nōn commovēbitur in aeternum, quī habitat in Jerosolimā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Montēs in circumitū ejus, et Dominus in circumitū populī suī, ex hōc nunc et usque in saeculum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quia nōn relinquet Dominus virgam peccātōrum super sortem jūstōrum, ut nōn extendant jūstī ad inīquitātem manūs suās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Benefac, Domine, bonīs, et rectīs corde.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Dēclīnantēs autem in obligātiōnēs, addūcet Dominus cum operantibus inīquitātem. Pax super Isrāēlem.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{125}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {In convertendō Dominus captīvitātem Siōnis, factī sumus sīcut consōlātī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Tunc replētum est gaudiō ōs nostrum, et lingua nostra exsultātiōne. Tunc dīcent inter gentēs, «~Magnificāvit Dominus facere cum eīs.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Magnificāvit Dominus facere nōbīscum~; factī sumus laetantēs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Converte, Domine, captīvitātem nostram, sīcut torrens in Austrō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quī sēminant in lacrimīs, in exsultātiōne metent.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Ientēs ībant et flēbant, mittentēs sēmina sua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Venientēs autem venient cum exsultātiōne, portantēs manipulōs suōs.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{126}{Canticum graduum Salomōnis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Nisī Dominus aedificāverit domum, in vānum labōrāvērunt, quī aedificant eam. Nisī Dominus custōdīverit cīvitātem, frūstrā vigilat, quī custōdit eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Vānum est vōbīs ante lūcem surgere, surgite postquam sēderitis, quī mandūcātis pānem dolōris. Quum dederit dīlectīs suīs somnum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Ecce hērēditās Dominī fīliī~; mercēs, fructus ventris.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Sīcut sagittae in manū potentis, ita fīliī excussōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Beātus vir quī implēvit dēsīderium suum ex ipsīs~; nōn confundētur quum loquētur inimīcīs suīs in portā.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{127}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Beātī omnēs, quī timent Dominum, quī ambulant in viīs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Labōrēs manuum tuārum quia mandūcābis~; beātus es, et bene tibī erit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Uxor tua sīcut vītis abundans, in lateribus domūs tuae. Fīliī tuī sīcut novellae olīvārum, in circumitū mensae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Ecce sīc benedīcētur homō, quī timet Dominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Benedīcat tibī Dominus ex Siōne, et videās bona Jerosolimae omnibus diēbus vītae tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Et videās fīliōs fīliōrum tuōrum, pācem super Isrāēlem.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{128}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Saepe expugnāvērunt mē ā juventūte meā, dīcat nunc Isrāel.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Saepe expugnāvērunt mē ā juventūte meā~; etenim nōn potuērunt mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Suprā dorsum meum fabricāvērunt peccātōrēs~; prolongāvērunt inīquitātem suam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Dominus jūstus concīdit cervīcēs peccātōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Confundantur et convertantur retrorsum omnēs, quī ōdērunt Siōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Fīant sīcut foenum tectōrum, quod priusquam ēvellātur exāruit,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {dē quō nōn implēvit manum suam quī metit, et sinum suum quī manipulōs colligit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Et nōn dixērunt quī praeterībant, «~Benedictiō Dominī super vōs~; benediximus vōbīs in nōmine Dominī.~»}


\psalmKathismaStasis{18}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{129}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Dē prōfundīs clāmāvī ad tē, Domine.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Domine, exaudī vōcem meam~; fīant aurēs tuae intendentēs in vōcem dēprecātiōnis meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {¿~Sī inīquitātēs observāverīs, Domine, Domine, quis sustinēbit~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quia apud tē propitiātiō est.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Propter lēgem tuam sustinuī tē, Domine~; sustinuit anima mea in verbō ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Spērāvit anima mea in Dominō ā custōdiā mātūtīnā usque ad noctem~; spēret Isrāel in Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Quia apud Dominum misericordia, et cōpiōsa apud eum redemptiō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Et ipse redimet Isrāēlem ex omnibus inīquitātibus ejus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{130}{Canticum graduum Dāvīd}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Domine nōn est exaltātum cor meum, neque ēlātī sunt oculī meī, neque ambulāvī in magnīs, neque in mīrābilibus super mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Sī nōn humiliter sentiēbam, sed exaltāvī animam meam, sīcut ablactātus est super mātre suā, ita retribūtiō in animā meā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Spēret Isrāel in Dominō, ex hoc nunc et usque in saeculum.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{131}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Mementō, Domine, Dāvid et omnis mansuētūdinis ejus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {sīcut jūrāvit Dominō~; vōtum vōvit Deō Jācōbis,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {«~Sī introīverō in tabernāculum domūs meae, sī ascenderō in lettum strātī meī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {sī dederō somnum oculīs meīs, et palpebrīs meīs dormītātiōnem,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {et requiem temporibus meīs, dōnec inveniam locum Dominō, tabernāculum Deō Jācōbis.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Ecce audīvimus eam in Efrātā~; invēnimus eam in campīs silvae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Introībimus in tabernāculum ejus~; adōrābimus in locō, ubi stetērunt pedēs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Surge Domine in requiem tuam, tū et arca sanctificātiōnis tuae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Sacerdōtēs tuī induantur jūstitiam, et sanctī tuī exsultent.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Propter Dāvid servum tuum, nōn āvertās faciem chrīstī tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Jūrāvit Dominus Dāvid vēritātem, et nōn frūstrābitur eam, «~Dē fructū ventris tuī pōnem super sēdem tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Sī custōdīverint fīliī tuī testāmentum meum, et testimōnia mea haec quae docēbō eōs, et fīliī eōrum usque in saeculum sedēbunt super sēdem tuam.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Quoniam ēlēgit Dominus Siōnem~; ēlēgit eam in habitātiōnem sibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Haec requiēs mea in saeculum saeculī~; hīc habitābō, quoniam ēlēgī eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Viduam ejus benedīcens benedīcem~; pauperēs ejus saturābō pānibus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Sacerdōtēs ejus induem salūtārī, et sanctī ejus exsultātiōne exsultābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Illūc prōdūcem cornū Dāvid~; parāvī lucernam chrīstō meō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Inimīcōs ejus induem confūsiōne~; super ipsum autem efflōrēbit sanctificātiō mea.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{132}{Canticum graduum Dāvīd}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Ecce quam bonum et quam jūcundum habitāre frātrēs in ūnum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Sīcut unguentum in capite, quod dēscendit in barbam, barbam Aarōnis, quod dēscendit in orram vestīmentī ejus~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {sīcut rōs Hermōnis, quī dēscendit in montem Siōnis. Quoniam illīc mandāvit Dominus benedictiōnem, et vītam usque in saeculum.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{133}{Canticum graduum}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Ecce nunc benedīcite Dominum, omnēs servī Dominī, quī stātis in domū Dominī, in ātriīs domūs Deī nostrī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {In noctibus extollite manūs vestrās in sancta, et benedīcite Dominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Benedīcat tē Dominus ex Siōne, quī fēcit caelum et terram.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{19}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{134}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudāte nōmen Dominī~; laudāte, servī, Dominum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {quī stātis in domū Dominī, in ātriīs domūs Deī nostrī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Laudāte Dominum, quia bonus Dominus~; psallite nōminī ejus, quoniam suāve.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quoniam Jācōbem ēlēgit sibī Dominus, Isrāēlem in possessiōnem sibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quia egō cognōvī quod magnus est Dominus, et Deus noster prae omnibus deīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Omnia quaecumque voluit Dominus fēcit, in caelō, in terrā, in marī, et in omnibus abissīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ēdūcens nūbēs ab extrēmō terrae, fulgura in pluviam fēcit~; quī prōdūcit ventōs dē tezsaurīs suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Quī percussit prīmōgenita Aegiptī ab homine usque ad pecus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Et mīsit signa, et prōdigia in mediō tuī, Aegipte~; in Pharaōnem, et in omnēs servōs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quī percussit gentēs multās, et occīsit rēgēs fortēs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Sehon rēgem Amorraeōrum, et Og rēgem Bāsānis, et omnia regna Chanaānis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Et dedit terram eōrum hērēditātem, hērēditātem Isrāēlī populō suō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Domine, nōmen tuum in aeternum~; Domine, memoriāle tuum in generātiōnem et generātiōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Quia jūdicābit Dominus populum suum, et in servīs suīs dēprecābitur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Simulācra Gentium argentum et aurum, opera manuum hominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Ōs habent, et nōn loquentur~; oculōs habent, et nōn vidēbunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Aurēs habent, et nōn audient~; neque enim est spīritus in ōre ipsōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Similēs illīs fīant quī faciunt ea, et omnēs quī confīdunt in eīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Domus Isrāēlis, benedīcite Dominō~; domus Aarōnis, benedīcite Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Domus Lēvī, benedīcite Dominō~; quī timētis Dominum, benedīcite Dominō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Benedictus Dominus ex Siōne, quī habitat in Jerosolimā.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{135}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēminī Dominō quoniam bonus, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Confitēminī Deō deōrum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Confitēminī Dominō dominōrum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quī facit mīrābilia magna sōlus, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quī fēcit caelōs in intellectū, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Quī firmāvit terram super aquās, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Quī fēcit lūmināria magna, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Sōlem in potestātem diēī, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Lūnam et stellās in potestātem noctis, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quī percussit Aegiptum cum prīmōgenitīs eōrum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Quī ēduxit Isrāēlem dē mediō eōrum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Et ēduxit Isrāēlem per medium ejus, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Et excussit Faraōnem, et virtūtem ejus in Marī Rubrō, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Quī trāduxit populum suum per dēsertum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Quī percussit rēgēs magnōs, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Et occīsit rēgēs fortēs, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Sehon rēgem Amorraeōrum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Et Og rēgem Bāsānis, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Et dedit terram eōrum hērēditātem, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Hērēditātem Isrāēlī servō suō, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Quia in humilitāte nostrā memor fuit nostrī, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}

\psalmVerse

\psalmVerse

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}27}
  {Confitēminī Dominō dominōrum, quoniam in aeternum misericordia ejus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{136}{Psalmus Dāvīdis Jēremīae}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Super flūmina Babilōnis, illīc sēdimus et flēvimus, quum recordārēmur Siōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {In salicibus in mediō ejus, suspendimus organa nostra,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {quia illīc interrogāvērunt nōs, quī captīvōs duxērunt nōs, verba cantiōnum, et quī abduxērunt nōs, himnum, «~Cantāte nōbīs dē canticīs Siōnis.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {¿~Quōmodō cantābimus canticum Dominī in terrā aliēnā~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Sī oblītus fuerō tuī, Jerosolima, oblīviōnī dētur dextera mea.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Adhaereat lingua mea faucibus meīs, sī nōn meminerō tuī~; sī nōn prōposuerō Jerosolimam in principiō laetitiae meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Memor estō, Domine fīliōrum Edōmis in diē Jerosolimae, quī dīcunt, «~Exinānīte, exinānīte usque ad fundāmentum in eā.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Fīlia Babilōnis misera~; beātus, quī retribuet tibī retribūtiōnem tuam, quam retribuistī nōbīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Beātus quī tenēbit, et allīdet parvulōs tuōs ad petram.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{19}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{137}{Ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Confitēbor tibī, Domine, in tōtō corde meō, quoniam audīvistī verba ōris meī. In conspectū angelōrum psallem tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Adōrābō ad templum sanctum tuum, et confitēbor nōminī tuō, super misericordiā tuā et vēritāte tuā~; quoniam magnificāvistī super omne, nōmen sanctum tuum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {In quācumque diē invocāverō tē, exaudī mē~; multiplicābis in animā meā virtūtem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Confiteantur tibī Domine omnēs rēgēs terrae, quia audīvērunt omnia verba ōris tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Et cantent in viīs Dominī, quoniam magna est glōria Dominī~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {quoniam excelsus Dominus, et humilia respicit, et alta ā longē cognōscit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Sī ambulāverō in mediō trībulātiōnis, vīvificābis mē~; super īram inimīcōrum meōrum extendistī manum tuam, et salvum mē fēcit dextera tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Dominus retribuet prō mē. Domine, misericordia tua in saeculum~; opera manuum tuārum nē dēspiciās.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{138}{In fīnem psalmus Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Domine probāvistī mē, et cognōvistī mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {tū cognōvistī sessiōnem meam et resurrectiōnem meam~; intellexistī cōgitātiōnēs meās dē longē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Sēmitam meam et fūniculum meum investīgāvistī, et omnēs viās meās praevīdistī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {quia nōn est sermō in linguā meā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Ecce, Domine, tū cognōvistī omnia, novissima et antīqua~; tū formāvistī mē, et posuistī super mē manum tuam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Mīrābilis facta est scientia tua ex mē~; confortāta est, et nōn poterō ad eam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {¿~Quō ībō ā Spīritū tuō, et quō ā faciē tuā fugiam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Sī ascenserō in caelum, tū illic es~; sī dēscenserō in infernum, ades.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Sī sumpserō pennās meās dīlūculō, et habitāverō in extrēmīs maris,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {etenim illūc manus tua dēdūcet mē, et tenēbit mē dextera tua.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Et dixī, «~Forsitan tenebrae conculcābunt mē, et nox illūminātiō mea in dēliciīs meīs~»,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {quia tenebrae nōn obscūrābuntur ā tē, et nox sīcut diēs illūminābitur~; sīcut tenebrae ejus, ita et lūmen ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Quia tū possēdistī rēnēs meōs~; suscēpistī mē dē uterō mātris meae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Confitēbor tibī, quia terribiliter magnificātus es~; mīrābilia opera tua, et anima mea cognōscit nimis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Nōn est occultātum os meum ā tē, quod fēcistī in occultō, et substantia mea in inferiōribus terrae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Imperfectum meum vīdērunt oculī tuī, et in librō tuō omnēs scrībentur~; diēs formābuntur, et nēmō in eīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Mihī autem nimis honōrificātī sunt amīcī tuī, Deus~; nimis confortātus est principātūs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Dīnumerābō eōs, et super arēnam multiplicābuntur~; exsurrexī, et adhūc sum tēcum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Sī occīserīs peccātōrēs, Deus~; virī sanguinum, dēclīnāte ā mē,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {quia dīcitis in cōgitātiōne, «~Accipient in vānitāte cīvitātēs tuās.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {¿~Nōnne quī ōdērunt tē, Domine, ōderam, et super inimīcōs tuōs tābēscēbam~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Perfectō odiō ōderam illōs, et inimīcī factī sunt mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}23}
  {Probā mē, Deus, et scītō cor meum~; interrogā mē, et cognōsce sēmitās meās.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}24}
  {Et vidē sī via inīquitātis in mē est, et dēdūc mē in viā aeternā.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{139}{In fīnem psalmus Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Ēripe mē Domine ab homine malō~; ā virō inīquō ēripe mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quī cōgitāvērunt inīquitātēs in corde~; tōtā diē constituēbant praelia.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Acūvērunt linguās suās sīcut serpentis~; venēnum aspidum sub labiīs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Custōdī mē, Domine, dē manū peccātōris, et ab hominibus inīquīs ēripe mē, quī cōgitāvērunt supplantāre gressūs meōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Abscondērunt superbī laqueum mihī, et fūnēs extendērunt in laqueum~; juxtā iter scandalum posuērunt mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Dixī Dominō, «~Deus meus es tū~; exaudī, Domine, vōcem dēprecātiōnis meae.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Domine, Domine, virtūs salūtis meae, obumbrāvistī super caput meum in diē bellī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Nē trādās mē, Domine, ā dēsīderiō meō peccātōrī~; cōgitāvērunt contrā mē~; nē dērelinquās mē, nē forte exaltentur.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Caput circumitūs eōrum~; labor labiōrum ipsōrum operiet eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Cadent super eōs carbōnēs~; in ignem dējiciēs eōs~; in miseriīs nōn subsistent.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {Vir linguōsus nōn dīrigētur in terrā~; virum injūstum mala capient in interitū.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Cognōvī quia faciet Dominus jūdicium inopis, et vindictam pauperum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Vērumtamen jūstī confitēbuntur nōminī tuō, et habitābunt rectī cum vultū tuō.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{19}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{140}{Psalmus Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Domine, clāmāvī ad tē, exaudī mē~; intende vōcī meae, quum clāmāverō ad tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Dīrigātur ōrātiō mea sīcut incensum in conspectū tuō~; ēlevātiō manuum meārum sacrificium vespertīnum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Pōne, Domine, custōdiam ōrī meō, et ōstium circumstantiae labiīs meīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Nōn dēclīnēs cor meum in verba malitiae, ad excūsandās excūsātiōnēs in peccātīs~; cum hominibus operantibus inīquitātem, et nōn commūnicābō cum ēlectīs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Corripiet mē jūstus in misericordiā, et increpābit mē~; oleum autem peccātōris nōn impinguet caput meum, quoniam adhūc et ōrātiō mea in benēplacitīs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Absorptī sunt junctī petrae jūdicēs eōrum~; audient verba mea quoniam potuērunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Sīcut crassitūdō terrae ērupta est super terram, dissipāta sunt ossa nostra secus infernum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Quia ad tē, Domine, Domine oculī meī~; in tē spērāvī, nōn auferās animam meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Custōdī mē ā laqueō, quem statūvērunt mihī, et ā scandalīs operantium inīquitātem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Cadent in rētiāculō ejus peccātōrēs~; singulāriter sum egō, dōnec transeam.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{141}{Intellēctus Dāvīdis quum esset in spēluncā ōrātiō}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Vōce meā ad Dominum clāmāvī, vōce meā ad Dominum dēprecātus sum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Effundō in conspectū ejus dēprecātiōnem meam, et trībulātiōnem meam ante ipsum prōnuntiō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {In dēficiendō ex mē spīritum meum, et tū cognōvistī sēmitās meās. In viā hāc quā ambulābam abscondērunt laqueum mihī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Consīderābam ad dexteram, et vidēbam, et nōn erat quī cognōsceret mē. Perīvit fuga ā mē, et nōn est quī requīrat animam meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Clāmāvī ad tē, Domine~; dixī, «~Tū es spēs mea, portiō mea in terrā vīventium.~»}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Intende ad dēprecātiōnem meam, quia humiliātus sum nimis. Līberā mē ā persequentibus mē, quia confortātī sunt super mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Ēdūc dē custōdiā animam meam ad confitendum nōminī tuō~; mē expectant jūstī dōnec retribuās mihī.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{142}{Psalmus Dāvīdis quandō persequēbātur eum Absalom fīlius ejus}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Domine exaudī ōrātiōnem meam~; auribus percipe obsecrātiōnem meam in vēritāte tuā~; exaudī mē in tuā jūstitiā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Et nōn intrēs in jūdicium cum servō tuō, quia nōn jūstificābitur in conspectū tuō omnis vīvens.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quia persecūtus est inimīcus animam meam~; humiliāvit in terrā vītam meam. Collocāvit mē in obscūrīs sīcut mortuōs saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Et anxiātus est super mē spīritus meus~; in mē turbātum est cor meum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Memor fuī diērum antīquōrum~; meditātus sum in omnibus operibus tuīs~; in factīs manuum tuārum meditābar.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Expandī manūs meās ad tē~; anima mea sīcut terra sine aquā tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Vēlōciter exaudī mē, Domine, dēfēcit spīritus meus. Nōn āvertās faciem tuam ā mē, et similis erō dēscendentibus in lacum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Audītam fac mihī māne misericordiam tuam, quia in tē spērāvī. Nōtam fac mihī viam in quā ambulem, quia ad tē levāvī animam meam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Ēripe mē dē inimīcīs meīs, Domine, ad tē confūgī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Docē mē facere voluntātem tuam, quia Deus meus es tū. Spīritus tuus bonus dēdūcet mē in terram rectam.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Propter nōmen tuum, Domine, vīvificābis mē. In aequitāte tuā ēdūcēs dē trībulātiōne animam meam,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {et in misericordiā tuā disperdēs inimīcōs meōs, et perdēs omnēs, quī trībulant animam meam, quoniam egō servus tuus sum.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{20}{1}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{143}{Psalmus Dāvīdis adversus Golīam}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Benedictus Dominus, Deus meus, quī docet manūs meās ad praelium, et digitōs meōs ad bellum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Misericordia mea, et refugium meum~; susceptor meus, et līberātor meus~; prōtector meus, et in ipsō spērāvī, quī subdit populum meum sub mē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Domine quid est homō, quia innōtuistī eī~? Aut fīlius hominis, quia reputās eum~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Homō vānitātī similis factus est~; diēs ejus sīcut umbra praeteriunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Domine inclīnā caelōs tuōs, et dēscende~; tange montēs, et fūmigābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Fulgurā coruscātiōnem, et dissipābis eōs~; ēmitte sagittās tuās, et conturbābis eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ēmitte manum tuam dē altō, ēripe mē, et līberā mē dē aquīs multīs, dē manū fīliōrum aliēnōrum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {quōrum ōs locūtum est vānitātem, et dextera eōrum dextera inīquitātis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Deus, canticum novum cantābō tibī~; in psaltēriō, decachordō psallem tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Quī dās salūtem rēgibus, quī redēmistī Dāvid servum tuum dē gladiō malignō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Ēripe mē, et ērue mē dē manū fīliōrum aliēnōrum, quōrum ōs locūtum est vānitātem, et dextera eōrum dextera inīquitātis,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {quōrum fīliī sīcut novellae plantātiōnēs in juventūte suā. Fīliae eōrum compositae~; circumornātae ut similitūdō templī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Prōmptuāria eōrum plēna, ēructantia ex hōc in illud. Ovēs eōrum foetōsae, abundantēs in ēgressibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Bovēs eōrum crassae. Nōn est ruīna māceriae, neque transitus, neque clāmor in platēīs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Beātum dixērunt populum, cui haec sunt~; beātus populus cujus Dominus Deus ejus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{144}{Laudātiō ipsī Dāvīdis}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Exaltābō tē, Deus meus rex, et benedīcem nōminī tuō in saeculum, et in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Per singulōs diēs benedīcem tibī, et laudābō nōmen tuum in saeculum, et in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Magnus Dominus, et laudābilis nimis, et magnitūdinis ejus nōn est fīnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Generātiō et generātiō laudābit opera tua, et potentiam tuam prōnuntiābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Magnificentiam glōriae sanctitātis tuae loquentur, et mīrābilia tua narrābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Et virtūtem terribilium tuōrum dīcent, et magnitūdinem tuam narrābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Memoriam abundantiae suāvitātis tuae ēructābunt, et jūstitia tua exsultābunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Miserātor et misericors Dominus~; patiens, et multum misericors.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Suāvis Dominus ūniversīs, et miserātiōnēs ejus super omnia opera ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Confiteantur tibī, Domine, omnia opera tua, et sanctī tuī benedīcant tibī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Glōriam regnī tuī dīcent, et potentiam tuam loquentur,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {ut nōtam faciant fīliīs hominum potentiam tuam, et glōriam magnificentiae regnī tuī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {Regnum tuum regnum omnium saeculōrum, et dominātiō tua in omnī generātiōne et generātiōnem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Fidēlis Dominus in omnibus verbīs suīs, et sanctus in omnibus operibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}15}
  {Allevat Dominus omnēs, quī corruunt, et ērigit omnēs ēlīsōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}16}
  {Oculī omnium in tē spērant, Domine, et tū dās ēscam illōrum in tempore opportūnō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}17}
  {Aperīs tū manum tuam, et implēs omne animal benedictiōne.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}18}
  {Jūstus Dominus in omnibus viīs suīs, et sanctus in omnibus operibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}19}
  {Prope est Dominus omnibus invocantibus eum, omnibus invocantibus eum in vēritāte.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}20}
  {Voluntātem timentium sē faciet, et dēprecātiōnem eōrum exaudiet, et salvōs faciet eōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}21}
  {Custōdit Dominus omnēs dīligentēs sē, et omnēs peccātōrēs disperdet.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}22}
  {Laudātiōnem Dominī loquētur ōs meum, et benedīcat omnis carō nōminī sanctō ejus in saeculum, et in saeculum saeculī.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{20}{2}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{145}{Allēlūia Aggaeī et Zacharīae}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudā, anima mea, Dominum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Laudābō Dominum in vītā meā~; psallem Deō meō quamdiū fuerō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Nōlīte confīdere in principibus, in fīliīs hominum, in quibus nōn est salūs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Exībit spīritus ejus, et revertētur in terram suam~; in illā diē perībunt omnēs cōgitātiōnēs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Beātus cujus Deus Jācōbis adjūtor ejus, spēs ejus in Dominō Deō ipsīus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {quī fēcit caelum et terram, mare, et omnia quae in eīs sunt, quī custōdit vēritātem in saeculum,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {facit jūdicium injūriam patientibus, dat ēscam ēsurientibus. Dominus solvit compedītōs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Dominus illūminat caecōs~; Dominus ērigit ēlīsōs~; Dominus dīligit jūstōs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Dominus custōdit advenās~; pūpillum et viduam suscipiet, et viās peccātōrum disperdet.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Regnābit Dominus in saecula~; Deus tuus, Siōn, in generātiōnem et generātiōnem.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{146}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudāte Dominum, quoniam bonus est psalmus~; Deō nostrō sit jūcunda, decōraque laudātiō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Aedificans Jerosolimam Dominus~; dispersiōnēs Isrāēlis congregābit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quī sānat contrītōs corde, et alligat contrītiōnēs eōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quī numerat multitūdinem stellārum, et omnibus eīs nōmina vocat.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Magnus Dominus noster, et magna virtūs ejus, et sapientiae ejus nōn est numerus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Suscipiens mansuētōs Dominus~; humilians autem peccātōrēs usque ad terram.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Praecinite Dominō in confessiōne~; psallite Deō nostrō in cittarā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Quī operit caelum nūbibus, et parat terrae pluviam~; quī prōdūcit in montibus foenum, et herbam servitūtī hominum~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {quī dat jūmentīs ēscam ipsōrum, et pullīs corvōrum invocantibus eum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {Nōn in fortitūdine equī voluntātem habēbit, nec in tībiīs virī benēplacitum erit eī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {Benēplacitum est Dominō super timentēs eum, et in eīs quī spērant super misericordiā ejus.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{147}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudā, Jerosolima, Dominum~; laudā Deum tuum, Siōn.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Quoniam confortāvit serās portārum tuārum~; benedixit fīliīs tuīs in tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Quī posuit fīnēs tuōs pācem, et adipe frūmentī satiat tē.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quī ēmittit ēloquium suum terrae~; vēlōciter currit sermō ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Quī dat nivem sīcut lānam~; nebulam sīcut cinerem spargit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Mittit cristallum suum sīcut buccellās~; ¿~ante faciem frīgoris ejus quis sustinēbit~?}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Ēmittet verbum suum, et liquefaciet ea~; flābit spīritus ejus, et fluent aquae.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {Quī adnuntiat verbum suum Jācōbī~; jūstitiās, et jūdicia sua Isrāēlī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {Nōn fēcit tāliter omnī nātiōnī, et jūdicia sua nōn manifestāvit eīs.}


\psalmKathismaStasis{20}{3}

\psalmChapterWithInscription{148}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudāte Dominum dē caelīs~; laudāte eum in excelsīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Laudāte eum, omnēs angelī ejus~; laudāte eum, omnēs virtūtēs ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Laudāte eum, sōl et lūna~; laudāte eum, omnēs stellae et lūmen.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Laudāte eum, caelī caelōrum, et aqua quae super caelōs sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Laudent nōmen Dominī~; quia ipse dixit, et facta sunt~; ipse mandāvit, et creāta sunt.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Statūvit ea in aeternum, et in saeculum saeculī~; praeceptum posuit, et nōn praeterībit.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {Laudāte Dominum dē terrā, dracōnēs et omnēs abissī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {ignis, grandō, nix, glaciēs, spīritus procellae, quae faciunt verbum ejus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {montēs et omnēs collēs, ligna fructifera et omnēs cedrī,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}10}
  {bēstiae et ūniversa pecora, serpentēs et volucrēs pennātae,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}11}
  {rēgēs terrae et omnēs populī, principēs et omnēs jūdicēs terrae,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}12}
  {juvenēs et virginēs, senēs cum jūniōribus,}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}13}
  {laudent nōmen Dominī, quia exaltātum est nōmen ejus sōlīus~; confessiō ejus super caelum et terram.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{0}14}
  {Et exaltāvit cornū populī suī~; himnus omnibus sanctīs ejus, fīliīs Isrāēlis, populō appropinquantī sibī.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{149}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Cantāte Dominō canticum novum~; laus ejus in ecclēsiā sanctōrum.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Laetētur Isrāel in eō, quī fēcit eum, et fīliī Siōnis exsultent in rēge suō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Laudent nōmen ejus in chorō~; in timpanō et psaltēriō psallant eī.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Quia benēplacitum est Dominō in populō suō, et exaltābit mansuētōs in salūtem.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Exsultābunt sanctī in glōriā~; laetābuntur in cubīlibus suīs.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Exaltātiōnēs Deī in gutture eōrum, et gladiī ancipitēs in manibus eōrum~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}7}
  {ad faciendam vindictam in nātiōnibus, increpātiōnēs in populīs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}8}
  {ad alligandōs rēgēs eōrum in compedibus, et nōbilēs eōrum in manicīs ferreīs~;}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}9}
  {ut faciant in eīs jūdicium conscrīptum~; glōria haec est omnibus sanctīs ejus. Allēlūia.}


\psalmChapterWithInscription{150}{Allēlūia}

\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}1}
  {Laudāte Dominum in sanctīs ejus~; laudāte eum in firmāmentō virtūtis ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}2}
  {Laudāte eum in virtūtibus ejus~; laudāte eum secundum multitūdinem magnitūdinis ejus.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}3}
  {Laudāte eum in sonō tubae~; laudāte eum in psaltēriō, et cittarā.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}4}
  {Laudāte eum in timpanō, et chorō~; laudāte eum in chordīs, et organō.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}5}
  {Laudāte eum in cimbalīs bene sonantibus~; laudāte eum in cimbalīs jūbilātiōnis.}


\psalmVerse
  {\phantom{00}6}
  {Omnis spīritus laudet Dominum. Allēlūia.}
